in cases where participation of international service providers is contemplated period of not less than four weeks should normally be allowed
tender documents should invariably reserve the procuring entity right without assigning any reason to reject any or all of the bids or cancel the tender process or abandon the procurement of the services or issue another tender for identical or similar services
contents of tender documents rule of gfr
the tender document has the following main sections
reading of the sections of the tender document will make the purpose and instructions clear section notice inviting tender nit and its appendix tender information summary tis section ii instructions to bidders itb section iii appendix to instructions to bidders aitb section iv general conditions of contract gcc section special conditions of contract scc section vi schedule of requirements section vii technical specifications and quality assurance section viii qualification and evaluation criteria financial bid boq excel sheet submission forms and formats including bid form cover letter bank guarantees and contract format etc
notice inviting tender nit is of legal importance since it is this part of the tender document that solicits offers from the bidders
the model nit format in mtd should be used to publish the tender notice
the notice inviting tender nit is crucial for attracting wide competition in the tender
the nit and its appendix tis must contain sufficient information in brief for prospective bidder to decide whether to participate in the tender and if he decides to participate how to go about it
to ensure competition the attention of all likely bidders for example registered vendors past suppliers and other known potential suppliers should be invited to the nit through letters
in the website may be programmed to generate these alerts automatically
in case of procurement through limited tender the nit may be uploaded on the gem as well as on cppp and procuring entity website with note saying this notice is being published for information only and is not an open invitation to quote in this limited tender
participation in this tender is by invitation only and is limited to the selected procuring entity registered suppliers
unsolicited offers are liable to be ignored
however suppliers who desire to participate in such tenders in future may apply for registration with procuring entity as per audit trails for the shall be maintained by the procurement portal
printouts may be taken only in case of tenders if required apart from ensuring maintenance of time stamped audit trail of
the complete details of the dates on which advertisements appeared on the website should be indicated when sending cases to higher authorities
instructions to bidders itb and its appendix aitb itb contain all relevant information as well as guidance to the prospective bidders regarding obtaining tender documents preparing and submitting responsive process of establishing the qualification credentials of the bidders as well as evaluation and comparison of tenders and award of contract but should not contain information on processes after the announcement of the award which should be covered in gcc for example the arbitration clause resolution of disputes and so on
itb also contains an overview of the contents of the tender document
instead of modifying itb every time any changes warranted by exceptional circumstances may be indicated with the prior approval of ca in separate appendix to itb aitb and itb may be included unchanged in every tender document
it should also be indicated therein that the provisions in the aitb shall supersede the corresponding provisions in the itb
general and special conditions of the contract gcc and scc the general conditions of contract gcc details the terms and conditions that would govern the resultant contract
gcc covers all information on aspects after the announcement of the tender award till the closure of the contract and dispute resolution
it should not cover any aspect up to the announcement of the award
instead of modifying the gcc every time any changes warranted by exceptional circumstances may be indicated in separate section special conditions of contract scc with the prior approval of the ca and gcc and may be included unchanged in every tender document
it is also to be indicated therein that the provisions in the scc will supersede the corresponding provisions in the gcc
schedule of requirements this section describes the list of goods required quantities delivery requirements destination and scope of supply concomitant accessories spare parts and incidental services
if there is no separate section on technical specifications ts and quality assurance qa then ts and qa may also be included here
it must be clarified whether the evaluation of financial bids would be done in schedule or on the total of all items in schedule and if there is more than one schedule whether the same would be done on the basis or the total of all schedules put together
technical specifications and quality assurance technical specifications and quality assurance lays down the technical specifications and quality assurance requirements of the goods required
it would also stipulate if required any compliance required by central and state pollution control boards
qualification criteria if it is intended to use qualification criteria to evaluate tender and determine whether bidder has the required qualifications to perform the contract successfully this point may be clearly specified in or as separate section of the tender document
the bidder must ensure that he provides convincing proof of having fulfilled these criteria
any criteria not specified in the tender can not be used for evaluation or qualification
post qualification criteria shall be based entirely upon the capability and resources required to perform the particular contract satisfactorily considering bidders experience and past performance capabilities with respect to personnel equipment and manufacturing facilities financial standing and relevant compliance with environmental protection environment management system
the quantity delivery and value of the procurement shall be kept in view while the post qualification criteria are fixed
there should be no post qualification criteria that would be advantageous to foreign manufactured goods at the cost of domestically manufactured goods
relaxation for the condition of prior turnover and prior experience may be for startups only to startups recognized by the department of industry internal trade dpiit subject to meeting quality technical specifications and making suitable provisions in the tender document rule of gfr
it is further clarified that such relaxation is not optional but has to be ensured except in case of procurement of items related to public safety health critical security operations and equipment etc where adequate justification exists for the procuring entity not to relax such criteria
submission forms and formats this section contains the relevant forms for tender submission various declarations by the bidder formats for the bank guarantee financial bid forms boq excel sheet exception and deviation forms contract forms and manufacturer authorisation form integrity pact if applicable and so on
financial bid boq excel sheet the procuring entity should select an appropriate format of boq from the eprocurement portal and upload it after filling up the entries for the complete schedule of requirements and various price components to enable the system to automatically calculate the price of bid to generate comparative tabulation of all bids
bidders are to upload only the downloaded boq in excel format after entering the relevant fields without altering deletion or modification of other portions of the excel sheet
the quoted price shall be considered to include all relevant financial implications including the scope of the goods to be supplied location of the bidder location of the consignee terms of delivery extant rules and regulations relating to taxes duties customs transportation environment labour of the bidder country and in india
uploading of tender documents mandatory rule of gfr
it is mandatory for all of the central government their attached and subordinate offices and bodies to publish their tender enquiries corrigenda thereof and details of bid awards online on the public procurement portal cppp and also on their website
these instructions apply to all tender enquiries requests for proposals requests for expressions of interest notice for registration or any other notice inviting bids or proposals in any form whether they are advertised issued to limited number of parties or single party
these instructions would not apply to the purchase of goods without quotations or the purchase of goods by the purchase committee
individual cases where confidentiality is required for reasons of national security would be exempted from the mandatory requirement
the decisions to exempt any case on the said grounds should be approved by the secretary of the department with the concurrence of the concerned financial advisor
in the case of autonomous bodies and statutory bodies approval of the head of the body with the concurrence of the head of the finance should be obtained in each such case
statistical information on the number of cases in which exemption was granted and the value of the concerned contract notified vide om pt
issued by department of expenditure dated should be intimated on quarterly basis to the ministry of finance department of expenditure
amendment of tender documents rule iii of gfr at any time prior to the date of submission of bids the procuring entity may or in response to clarification sought by prospective bidder directly or in conference amend tender documents by issuing corrigendum
copies of such amendment modification should be uploaded on the portal and procuring entity own website
in case of tenders the copies of such amendment modification are to be simultaneously despatched free of cost by to all the parties who have already purchased the tender documents and copies of such amendments are also to be prominently attached in the unsold sets of the tender documents which are available for sale
when the changes the requirement significantly and when there is not much time left for the bidders to respond to such amendments and prepare revised tender the time and date of submission of tenders are also to be suitably extended not less than days as per para below
extension of deadline of bid submission
to give sufficient time to bidders to prepare and submit their bids the procuring entity may or based on justifiable request of bidder or due to significant modification of tender documents as per para above extend the time and date of submission of tenders suitably not less than three days along with suitable changes in the corresponding for receipt of tender bid validity period etc and validity period of the corresponding security
depending on the situation such an amendment may also need fresh publication adopting the same procedure as for publication of the original tender enquiry
of bids in case of lack of response the gem should not provide anybody including the procuring entity with the bid count before the tender opening time even at their request
the eprocurement gem may facilitate the procuring entity in specifying the minimum number of bids considered sufficient and the number of days for automatic extension of bid opening not less than days at the time of tender upload
the system shall declare in the tender details that in case of low competition without specifying the number the tender closing time shall be automatically extended by the specified number of days
if bids received till the bid opening time are less than the specified minimum bids the system should automatically extend only once the tender opening by the specified number of days without seeking any input from or sharing any information with anyone including the procuring entity
purchasers and bidders shall only be informed that due to less competition the tender closing time has been extended up to date and time
however this automatic extension of bid opening shall be done only once not repeatedly
if procuring entity wants to go ahead even with low competition due to urgency they may mention one as the minimum bid
so that if no bid is received the tender is automatically extended otherwise it is not
gem and eprocurement portals shall update their systems accordingly
availability and cost of tender documents rule of gfr tender documents should preferably be sold or available for download after the date and time of the start of availability till the deadline for availability as mentioned in the tender document say up to date of opening of tenders and this should be clearly indicated in the documents
the organisation should also post the complete tender document on the website and permit prospective bidders to make use of the document downloaded from the website
normally no tender document fee should be charged
in exceptional cases procuring entity may fix bare minimum cost of tender documents to defray the effort of preparing documents drawings etc
the cost of the tender document is to be submitted to the authority nominated therein by the prospective bidder in the form of demand draft pay online payment gateway
firms that are eligible for exemption from the tender document cost such as mses and procuring entity registered units for relevant items and monetary limit have to upload scanned copies of documents in support of this exemption
participation of bidders
eligibility criteria the tender document may lay down eligibility criteria for more details refer to the mtd for procurement of goods for participating in the tender process restrictions on participation by bidders relating to type of commercial entity the bidders must be private or public registered entity insolvency conflict of interest class of bidders as per make in india order bidders from countries having land borders with india etc
except for the eligibility criteria participation shall be open to all bidders in global tender enquiries
in the case of the second stage of two stage bidding or pqb or limited tenders participation shall be open only to such bidders who have been previously shortlisted or specifically invited
purchase preference policies the procuring entity may reserve its right to grant preferences to eligible bidders under various government directives policies relating to make in india msme etc
conflict of interest bidders having conflict of interest shall not be eligible to participate in the tender process unless the conflict stemming from such relationship has been resolved in manner acceptable to the procuring entity throughout the tender process and execution of the contract
please also refer to para above
the bidder shall be considered to have conflict of interest in this tender process and execution of the resultant contract in the following situations if its personnel have close personal financial or business with any personnel of the procuring entity who are directly or indirectly related to the procurement or execution process of the contract which can affect the decision of the procuring entity directly or indirectly the bidder or his allied provided services for the need procurement of the tender process in which it is participating please refer to para for clarification please see definition in procurement glossary section need assessment preparation of cost detailed project report dpr principal can authorize only one agent and an agent should not represent or quote on behalf of more than one principal
however this shall not debar more than one authorised distributor or without the oem from quoting equipment manufactured by an original equipment manufacturer oem in procurements under proprietary article certificate or bidder participates in more than one bid in this tender process
participation in any capacity by bidder including the participation of bidder as jv member or in another bid or in more than one bid shall result in the disqualification of all bids in which he is party
however this does not limit the participation of an entity as in more than one bid if he is not bidding independently in his own name or as member of jv
agents of supplier except in the case of cots items when firm sends quotation for an item manufactured by some different company the firm is also required to attach in its quotation the manufacturer authorisation certificate and manufacturer confirmation of extending the required warranty support for that product in addition to the bidders confirmation to the required warranty as per formats given in tender documents
this is necessary to ensure quotation from responsible party offering genuine product backed by warranty obligation from the concerned manufacturer
in the case of large contracts especially capital equipment the manufacturer authorisation must be insisted upon on basis not general by clearly declaring it in the tender documents
and conferences rule of gfr
inviting tender nit conference market consultation in complex and innovative procurement cases or where the procuring entity may not have the required knowledge to formulate tender provisions conference before publishing nit may help the procuring entity in obtaining inputs from the industry
such conferences should be widely publicised so that different potential suppliers can
all inputs received from the probable bidders in such conference shall be minuted and requirements finalised with the approval of the technical committee if formed by the competent authority
in more complex large and project tendering with eoi would be more appropriate and transparent
please refer to para above
conference in case of turnkey contract and sophisticated and costly equipment large works and complex consultancy assignments suitable provision shall be kept in the tender documents for one or more conferences after the nit and tender documents have been published for clarifying doubts if any and for ensuring level playing field relating to the specifications and other allied details
participation in the conference may be restricted to prospective bidders who have downloaded the tender document
participation is not mandatory
however if bidder chooses not to or fails to participate in the conference or does not notified under para vide om issued by department of expenditure dated submit written query it shall be assumed that they have no issues regarding the commercial conditions
the date and time for such meeting should normally be after to fifteen to days of the issue of the tender document and should be specified therein
the date and time by which the written queries for the must reach the authority and the last date for registration for participation in the conference are also mentioned in the tender document days before the date of the conference if not specified
the conference may also be held online at the discretion of the procuring entity
timelines for response to the conference replies to questions issue of minutes of the conference corrigenda etc should be mandatorily mentioned in the tender document and complied with
delegates participating in the conference must provide photo identity and an authorization letter as per the specified format from their principals otherwise they shall not be allowed to participate
after the conference minutes of the conference shall be published on the procuring entity portal within seven days of the conference
if required clarification letter and corrigendum to the tender document as per para shall be issued containing amendments to various provisions of the tender document which shall form part of the tender document
to give reasonable time to the prospective bidders to take such clarifications into account in preparing their bids the procuring entity may suitably extend as necessary the deadline for the bid submission as per para
clarification of tender documents prospective bidder requiring clarification on the tender documents may ask questions in electronically from the contact person as mentioned in the tender document provided the questions are raised before the clarification end date mentioned therein or if not mentioned before days of the deadline for the bid submission
this deadline shall not be extended in case of any intervening holidays
response will be sent in digitally to the clarifications sought at least days prior to the date of opening of the tenders
only material queries and their responses shall be uploaded on the website without revealing the identity of the bidder making the query
when the response to clarification changes the requirement significantly and when there is not much time left for the bidders to respond to such responses the time and date of submission of tenders may also be suitably extended not less than days as per para above
amendments modifications to bids by bidders the bidder after submitting its bid is permitted to it superseding earlier bid so long such revised bid is received duly sealed and marked like the original bid up to the deadline of submission of bids
resubmission of bid shall require uploading all documents including the financial bid afresh
the system shall consider only the last bid submitted as valid bid
the bidder may withdraw his bid before the bid submission deadline and it shall be marked as withdrawn and shall not be opened during the bid opening
any such action after that deadline is not permitted
derogation of bid in any respect by its bidders between the deadline for submission of bids and the expiration of the period of bid validity his bid emd shall be forfeited besides imposition of any other punitive remedy available to the procuring entity
in such cases tender evaluation shall be proceeded with in terms of para below
marking of bids in tenders
the tender document should indicate the manner of uploading of bids
in the case of tenders the total number of bid copies for example duplicate or triplicate and so on required to be submitted should be specified
the bidder is to seal the original and each copy of the bid in separate envelopes duly marking the same as original duplicate and so on and print the address of the purchasing office and the tender reference number on the envelopes
further the sentence not to be opened before the due date and time of tender opening is also to be printed on these envelopes
the inner envelopes are then to be put inside bigger outer envelope which will also be duly sealed marked and so on as above
if the outer envelope is not sealed and marked properly as above the procuring entity does not assume any responsibility for its misplacement premature opening late opening and so on
submission of bids
uploading bids in eprocurement
different eprocurement may have different provisions but the following is the generic description the procuring entity is neither party nor principal in the relationship between bidder and the organisation hosting the portal hereinafter called the portal
bidders must acquaint and train themselves with the rules regulations procedures and implied agreements of the portal
bidders intending to participate in the bid shall be required to register with the portal
bidder must comply with the conditions of the eprocurement portal including registration compatible digital signature certificate dsc etc
in the case of downloaded documents bidder must not make any changes to the contents of the documents while uploading except for filling in the required information
any complaint regarding downloading tender documents and uploading bids on the portal may be addressed to the portal help desk
in case of conflict between the provisions of the portal and the tender document provisions of the portal shall prevail
bidders may study the resources provided by the portal for bidders
bids must be uploaded by the submission deadline mentioned in the tender document
if the office happens to be closed on the deadline to submit the bids as specified above this deadline shall not be extended
only one copy of the bid can be uploaded and bidder shall digitally sign all statements documents and certificates uploaded by him owning sole and complete responsibility for their authenticity as per the provisions of the it act as amended from time to time
regarding the protected price schedule excel format the bidder shall write his name in the space provided in the specified location only
bidder shall type rates in the figure only in the rate column of respective item without any blank cell or zero these portals must be compliant with guidelines for compliance to quality requirements of eprocurement gcqe july issued by systems standardisation testing and quality certification stqc directorate an attached office of the ministry of electronics and information technology meity government of india
values in the rate column and without any modification of other portions of the excel sheet
if space is inadequate bidder may upload additional documents under additional documents in the bid cover content
the date and time of the server clock which is also displayed on the bidders dashboard shall be used as the reference time for deciding the closing time of bid submission
bidders are advised to ensure they submit their bid within the deadline and time of bid submission taking the server clock as reference failing which the portal shall not accept the bids
no request on the account that the server clock was not showing the correct time and that particular bidder could not submit their bid because of this shall be entertained
failure or defects on the internet or heavy traffic at the server shall not be accepted as reason for complaint
the procuring entity shall not be responsible for any failure malfunction or breakdown of the electronic system used during the process
the bidder should ensure the correctness of the bid before uploading and take printout of the submission summary to confirm the successful bid upload
all bids uploaded by bidder to the portal shall be automatically encrypted
the encrypted bid can only be opened by the authorised persons on or after the due date and time
bidder must upload scanned copies of originals or copies of originals as specified
the bidder should ensure the legibility of the scanned documents uploaded by him
the procuring entity reserves its right to call for verification originals of all such documents from the bidders at any stage of evaluation especially from the successful bidder before the issue of letter of award loa
if so specified in the tender document originals or copies of originals as specified therein of specified scanned uploaded documents must be physically submitted before the deadline specified for it before the bid submission deadline if not so specified sealed in double cover and acknowledgement must be obtained before the bid submission deadline at the mentioned venue
failure to do so is likely to result in the bid being rejected
if the office is closed on the deadline for the physical submission of originals it shall stand extended to the next working day at the same time and venue
no manual bids shall be made available or accepted for submission in except for originals of scanned copies as per above
submission of bids in offline tender process in offline tenders receipt and custody of bids shall be done transparently to maintain the credibility of the process
the following guidelines should be adhered to for receipt and custody of bids the technical and financial proposals shall be submitted at the same time
to safeguard the integrity of the process the technical and financial proposals shall be submitted in separate sealed envelopes and kept in an outer sealed envelope
the procuring entity shall maintain tender boxes for receiving the bids at suitable locations which would facilitate security and easy access for bidders
if required tender boxes should be separate for each day of the week of tender opening and should be sealed by the bid opening committee boc of the day
the tender box shall have two locks
the key of one lock will be with the head of the office and the other key with the official nominated by him bids received by courier shall be deposited in the tender box by the dispatch section till the date and time of bid opening
bids sent by telex cable or facsimile are to be ignored and rejected
and for bids that can not be dropped into tender boxes the officials authorised to receive such bids shall maintain proper records and provide signed receipt with the date and time to the bearer of the bid
he will also sign on the cover duly indicating the date and time of receipt of the tender
names and designations of at least two such authorised officers should be mentioned in the tender documents
bid security scan of the original bid bsd should be uploaded along with bids
bids not complying with these provisions shall be rejected
in tenders bid security or if permitted bid securing declaration bsd must accompany the bid as per instructions in the tender document
bid validity bid shall remain valid for the period mentioned in the tender document days if not so specified
bid that is valid for shorter period shall be rejected as nonresponsive
in case the day up to which the bids are to remain valid falls on or is subsequently declared closed day for the procuring entity the bid validity shall automatically be deemed to be extended upto the next working day
the validity period should not be unreasonably long as keeping the tender unconditionally valid for acceptance for longer period entails the risk of getting higher prices from the bidders
please see para below for an extension of the bid validity period
immediately after the deadline for bid submission the procuring entity shall proceed to the bid opening
if the specified date of bid opening falls on is subsequently declared holiday or closed day for the procuring entity the bids shall be opened at the appointed time on the next working day
in offline tenders the boc shall comprise one officer each from the procuring entity and integrated finance
in all tenders uploaded by bidders are received safeguarded and opened online on the portal as detailed in appendix
in offline tenders receipt and custody of bids shall be done transparently to maintain the credibility of the process
the following guidelines should be adhered to for receipt and custody of bids the authorised representatives of bidders who intend to attend the tender opening in slte are to bring letters of authority from the corresponding bidder with them
the prescribed format for the letter of authority for attending the bid opening should be given in the tender document
all activities should be carried out demonstrably before such gathering
the prescribed format for the bid opening attendance sheet and report is given in annexure at prescheduled date and time the boc of the day should get the tender box opened after ensuring and demonstrating that the seal on the box has not been tampered with
all bids should be collected from the tender box
bids for tenders not opening on that day should be put back into the box and the box resealed
sometimes tenders are dropped wrongly into this tender box
such wrongly dropped tenders with appropriate endorsement should be put into the appropriate box or sent to the tender committee tc concerned if the date of opening is over
the bids for different tenders opening on the day including oversized bids which were submitted to designated officers should be sorted and count for each tender should be announced and recorded particularly noting any of bids
boc should ensure and demonstrate that bid envelopes are duly sealed and untampered
late bids should be separately counted but kept aside and not opened
in the case of an advertised tender enquiry or limited tender enquiry late bids that is bids received after the specified date and time for receipt of bids should not be considered rule of gfr the technical bids will be opened on the date and the financial proposals shall remain sealed and shall be opened publicly in due course of time only for those firms that have technically qualified
after opening every tender shall be numbered serially say if it is the third bid out of total initialled and dated on the first page by the boc
each page of the price schedule or letter attached to it shall also be similarly initialled particularly the prices delivery period and so on which shall also be circled and initialled along with the date
any other page containing significant information should also be dealt with similarly
blank pages if any should be crossed out across and marked accordingly by the boc
the original and duplicate if any copies in tender set are to be marked accordingly by the boc of left unfilled in tenders if any shall be initialled along with the date and time and numbered by the officials opening the tenders and the total number of such noticed alterations or the absence of any alteration should be explicitly marked on the first page of the bid
wherever is written only in figures the boc should write them in words
all should be similarly circled numbered and signed
in the absence of any blanks the remark no corrections noted should be written
similarly the absence of discounts should be marked with no discounts noted the boc is to announce the salient features of the tenders such as description and specification of the goods quoted price terms of delivery delivery period discount if any whether emd furnished or not and any other distinctive feature of the tender for the information of the representatives attending the tender opening
clarifications by the bidders shall not be allowed or recorded during the bid opening
boc has no authority to reject any tender at the tender opening stage proper sealing and codification need to be done on reference samples as well for samples that accompany the
these should be kept for reference under lock and key
details should be recorded in the sample register maintained in the opening section
financial instruments should be noted in the bid opening and handed over to the finance section for safe custody and monitoring
bid opening report containing the names of the bidders serial number wise and salient features of the tenders as read out during the public opening of tenders will be prepared by the tender opening officers and duly signed by them along with the date and time
the tenders that have been opened the list of the representatives attending the tender opening and the bid opening report are to be handed over to the nominated procuring officer and an acknowledgement shall be obtained from him
please note that as detailed in para for sample along with the bid for evaluation is strictly discouraged
exceptions to an open tender process are abused leading to processes
rigorously follow the conditions under which open tendering can be dispensed with
when are used the process of preparation of may be transparent and all eligible firms may not be included and some ineligible firms may get included
registration of all major procuring departments must keep list of registered bidders for use in restricted tendering
publicise even restricted bids on your website
bidders for slte may be transparently selected with the approval of ca
criteria pqb has the quality requirements and neither be very the entry of bidders
these criteria should be lay down criteria when pqb tendering is down
similar procedure shall later be followed during financial bid opening in case of bidding
objectives of transparency in eprocurement are amply served if data relating to the tender and award of contract are accessible to the public
as far as the bidders who have participated in tender participating bidders for transparency comparative summary of technical compliance details and of financials bids including qcbs calculations wherever applicable should also be accessible to them but not necessarily to the public at large unless sought and if permissible under the rti act
bidders may have genuine concerns about and operational trade secrets if their full technical and financial bids are accessible to their competitors or the public at large
this concern may get aggravated in complicated consultancy procurements
financial bids should not be made accessible to the public at large and call needs to be taken based on the sensitivity of details in the bids to restrict access of even participating bidders to full financial bids of their competitors
the decision of procuring entity to share or not share the full technical bids with other participating bidders should be clearly brought out in the tender documents
however clause may be added to the tender documents reserving the right of the procuring entity and the eprocurement portal to provide access to bidders financial bids to other participating bidders in addition to the comparative summary of technical and financial bids of all participating bidders
invitation to tender an open bid is not well publicised or gives insufficient time thereby restricting the number of bidders that participate
publicity and adequate time for bid submission must be ensured
approval should be obtained for shorter bid submission period
evaluation criteria are not set from the beginning or are not objective or not clearly stated in the tender documents thereby making them prone to being abused
objective relevant and clearly stated evaluation criteria must be specified in the chapter forms of securities prices payment terms and price variations
forms of security bid security rule of gfr
to safeguard against bidder withdrawing or altering his bid during the bid validity period in the case of advertised ote and gte tenders or special limited tender enquiry bid security also known as earnest money deposit emd is to be obtained from the bidders along with their
the amount of bid security should ordinarily range between two to five per cent of the estimated value of the goods to be procured
the amount of bid security rounded off to the nearest thousands of rupees as determined by the procuring entity is to be indicated in the tender documents
bid security may be obtained in the form of insurance surety account payee demand draft banker cheque or bank guarantee including guarantee from any of the commercial banks or payment online in an acceptable form
in case the bid security is more than threshold rupees five lakh and in case of foreign bidders in gte tenders it may be in the form of bank guarantee in equivalent foreign exchange amount in case of gte confirmed from any of the commercial banks in india in an acceptable form
the bid security is normally to remain valid for period of days beyond the final bid validity period
in place of bid security procuring entities after seeking approval from the competent authority may consider asking bidders to submit bid securing declaration bsd accepting that if they withdraw or modify their bids during the period of validity or if they are awarded the contract and they fail to submit performance security or to sign the contract before the deadline defined in the tender documents it shall be considered as violation of code on integrity and they shall be suspended for the time period specified in the bsd from being eligible to submit for contracts with the procuring entity
in appropriate cases submission of the bid security may be exempted with the competent authority ca approval especially in the case of tenders limited tenders and procurements directly from the manufacturer or authorised agents bidders that are currently registered and will also continue to remain registered during the bid validity period with the concerned procuring entity
micro and small enterprises mses as defined in the mse procurement policy issued by the department of micro small and medium enterprises msme and registered startups as recognized by the department for promotion of industry and internal trade dpiit please refer to para are exempt from payment of emd
in case the bidder falls into these categories the bidder should furnish certified copy of its valid registration details
except for mses this exemption is valid for the trade group and monetary value of registration only
vide om no pt
chapter forms of securities prices payment terms and price variations
bidder bid security shall be forfeited if the bidder withdraws or amends its bid or impairs or derogates from the tender in any respect within the period of validity of the tender or if the successful bidder fails to furnish the required performance security or to sign the contract within the specified period
bid securities of the unsuccessful bidders should be returned to them as soon as possible after the expiry of the final bid validity period and at the latest by the day after the award of the contract
bid security should be refunded to the successful bidder upon receipt of performance security
however in the case of or tendering bid securities of unsuccessful bidders during the first stage technical evaluation should be returned within days of declaration of the result of the first stage technical evaluation performance security rule of gfr
to ensure due performance of the contract performance security or performance bank guarantee pbg or security deposit sd is to be obtained from the successful bidder awarded the contract
unlike contracts of works and plants in the case of contracts for goods the need for performance security depends on the market conditions and commercial practice for the particular kind of goods
performance security should be for an amount of three to five per cent to for works of the value of the contract as specified in the tender
the procuring entity may stipulate an upper ceiling for the performance security amount
for an illustrative example the ceiling can be rs lakhs for tenders upto rs crores and rs crore for tenders above rs cr but below rs cr
for tenders of higher value than this the procuring entity may decide the amount of performance security but not less than rs cr mentioned above
however procuring entities are free to decide their own upper limits for performance security with the approval of competent authority and finance concurrence based on their perception of performance risks vis need for competition
performance security may be furnished in the form of an insurance surety account payee demand draft from commercial bank bank guarantee including from any of the commercial banks in india or online payment in an acceptable form safeguarding the purchaser interest in all respects
in the case of gte tenders the performance security should be in the same currency as the contract and must conform to the uniform rules for demand guarantees urdg an international convention regulating international
unlike the procurement of works in the procurement of goods the concept of taking part of the performance guarantee as money retained from the first or progressive bills of the supplier is not acceptable
submission of performance security is not necessary for tender value upto rupees lakh
set of rules developed by the international chamber of commerce first adopted in
the latest version urdg provides framework for harmonising international trading practices and establishes rules for independent guarantees and among trading partners for securing payment and performance in worldwide commercial contracts
procuring entity may exempt the following entities on their specific requests or otherwise from submission of performance security
ministries departments attached and subordinate offices autonomous bodies oem in whose favour pac in tenders issued against pac
performance security is to be furnished by specified date generally fourteen to days after notification of the award depending on the amount and it should remain valid for period of sixty or any other period mentioned in the tender documents days beyond the date of completion of all contractual obligations of the supplier including warranty obligations
in the case of goods contracts rate contracts and other contracts spanning over multiple years procuring entities may consider proportionately reducing performance security in proportion to the balance contract period wherever feasible instead of retaining the full performance security over the complete contract period which may be of years or may be more
the performance security will be forfeited and credited to the procuring entity account in the event of breach of contract by the contractor
it should be refunded to the contractor without interest after he duly performs and completes the contract in all respects full performance security should be forfeited even if the contractor has partially executed the work but not later than sixty days of completion of all such obligations including the warranty under the contract
the senior officers should monitor the return of performance securities and delays should be avoided
if feasible the details of these securities may be listed in the website of the procuring entity to make the process transparent and visible
insurance surety bond isb an insurance surety bond isb is agreement that provides financial assurance to one party the beneficiary by another party the surety or bonding company on behalf of third party the principal
isb ensures that the principal fulfils their contractual obligations
unlike bank guarantee it is type of insurance product and does not require deposit of collateral amount by the principal with the surety
here are the key components
principal the principal is the party that obtains the surety bond
the principal is typically the contractor or service provider who provides the performance security to the
beneficiary the beneficiary is the party procuring entity that requires the insurance surety bond
the beneficiary seeks financial protection in case the principal fails to meet their obligations
surety insurer the surety insurer is the bond issuing entity bank or insurance company that issues the bond
they act as guarantor assuring the beneficiary that the principal will perform as promised
if the principal defaults the surety insurer assesses the extent of default and determines the amount payable under the bond
if the principal does not pay within days the surety insurer pays within calendar days of receiving the necessary documentation
there is no bar from taking performance security from cpses electronic bank guarantee
background electronic bank guarantee is dematerialised bank guarantee processed on national services limited nesl an information utility registered with the insolvency and bankruptcy board of india under the aegis of the insolvency and bankruptcy code
it handles all lifecycle events of execution by the issuing bank intimation to and verification by the beneficiary amendment invocation or release by the beneficiary cancellation etc
the facility is available including days
beneficiaries and banks can continue to use their own bg templates
all bidders may be encouraged to submit instead of traditional bank guarantees
creation of the procuring entity should ensure that the contractor is informed in the tender documents of its unique identity number uin which can be allotted by its bank and email id
clause regarding may be included in the tender acknowledging and accepting the use of as valid form of bank guarantee for the tender process
the procuring entity may reserve the right to verify the authenticity of bgs and take necessary actions in case of discrepancies
the uin and email id of the beneficiary are specified by the issuing bank when creating the on the nesl portal upon being approached by the contractor
on creation of it is stored on the nesl portal
intimation to beneficiary nesl shall send notification to the email id of the beneficiary provided by the issuing bank as well as the beneficiary registered email id during issuance or subsequent event of invocation cancellation etc
the procuring entity can receive the email notification without registration but such an email shall not have the document attachment
the issuing bank can also arrange to forward the to the beneficiary through the applicant or any other mechanism
registration and login beneficiaries and their authorised representatives must register with nesl using uin and email id
they must log in to the nesl portal using the same details to view download verify or invoke the
integration with government procurement portals cppp gem state govt procurement portals is being explored to facilitate access without needing to log into the nesl portal
easy verification verification of the stored in nesl is sufficient and verification with the issuing bank is not required
this is significant benefit for procuring entities
invocation and release the process through nesl facilitates beneficiaries submitting requests for invocation or any other consents through digitally signed submission in the nesl portal without the need to approach the issuing bank
warranty bank guarantee in the case of works and capital equipment there is usually defect clause against defects arising from design material workmanship or any omission on the part of the contractor during specified period of months from the date of commissioning or the date of dispatch in case of goods whichever is earlier
in such cases the performance guarantee is to be valid upto sixty days beyond the warranty period
it is normally permissible in such situation to allow the performance guarantee to be valid upto sixty days beyond the commissioning period and the contractor may be allowed to submit fresh warranty bank guarantee of ten per cent of the value of the goods in the currency of the contract valid upto sixty days beyond the warranty period
in such cases the performance guarantee is to be returned only after satisfactory commissioning and receipt of such warranty bank guarantee
in the procurement of goods other than capital equipment and in the case of capital goods say up to rupees one lakh warranty clause is not called for
verification of bank guarantees
bank guarantees submitted by the as securities need to be immediately verified from the issuing bank before acceptance
there may not be any need to get the bank guarantee vetted by finance authority if it is in the specified format
guidelines for verification of bgs submitted by the contractors against performance payments and for various other purposes are as follows bg shall be as per the prescribed formats
the bg contains the name designation and code number of the bank officer signing the guarantee the address and other details including telephone no
of the controlling officer of the bank are obtained from the branch of the bank issuing the bg this should be included in all bgs the confirmation from the issuing branch of the bank is obtained in writing through registered speed sfms on the official portal of the procuring entity
the bank should be advised to confirm the issuance of the bgs specifically quoting the letter of procuring entity on the printed official letterhead of the bank indicating the address and other details including telephone nos
of the bank and the name designation and code number of the officer confirming the issuance of the bg pending receipt of confirmation as above confirmation can also be obtained with the help of the responsible officer at the field office which is close to the issuing branch of the bank who should personally obtain the confirmation from the issuing branch of the bank and forward the confirmation report to the concerned procuring entity
bank guarantees either received in physical form or electronic form should be verified for their genuineness following the prescribed method for the same and the organisations should do due diligence on the genuineness of the bank guarantees before acceptance of the same
corporate guarantee or indemnity bond shall not be accepted for bid security emd or performance security or in lieu of any other bank guarantee for advance warranty obligations
please note the ease with which an can be verified as shown in para above
safe custody and monitoring of emds performance securities and other instruments suitable mechanism for safe custody and monitoring of emds performance securities and other instruments should be developed and implemented by each procuring entity
the departments shall also make institutional arrangements for taking all necessary actions on time for extension or encashment or refund of emds and performance securities as the case may be
monitoring should also include monthly review of all bank guarantees and other instruments expiring in the next three months along with review of the progress of the corresponding contracts
extension of bank guarantees and other instruments where warranted should be sought immediately and implemented within their validity period
bank guarantee should never be handed over to the supplier for propose of extension of validity
such system of monitoring of securities and other instruments may be computerised with automatic alerts about lapse of validity etc
the elements of price included in the quotation of bidder depend on the nature of the goods to be supplied and the allied services to be performed the location of the supplier the location of the user terms of delivery extant rules and regulations about taxes duties and so on of the seller country and the buyer country
in the case of indigenous goods the main elements of price may include raw material production cost overhead packing and forwarding charges margin of profit transit insurance excise duty and other taxes and duties as applicable
in the case of imported goods in addition to elements of price similar to the above other than excise duty and taxes there may be elements of customs duty import duty landing and clearing charges and commission to indian agents
further depending on the nature of the goods whether domestic or imported there may be cost elements towards installation and commissioning operator training and so on
elements of price where the price has several components such as the price of the goods cost of installation and commissioning operators training and so on bidders should be asked to furnish cost indicating the applicable prices and taxes for each of such components along with the overall price
the payment schedule and terms will be linked to this cost
currency the tender documents are to specify the currency currencies in which the tenders are to be priced
for domestic bidding regardless of whether the bidder is foreign or indian the currency of the bid and payment should be entirely in indian rupees
in gte global tender enquiry foreign bidders have the flexibility to quote prices and receive payments in either indian rupees or freely convertible currencies such as us dollars euros pound sterling yen other relevant or combination thereof
as general rule domestic bidders are to quote and accept their payment in indian currency indian agents of foreign suppliers are to receive their agency commission in indian currency costs of imported goods which are directly imported against the contract may be quoted in foreign currency currencies and paid accordingly in that currency and the portion of the allied work and services which are to be undertaken in india like installation and commissioning of equipment are to be quoted and paid in indian currency
payment to suppliers in supply contract the delivery of goods is the essence of the contract for the purchaser
similarly receiving timely payment for the supplies is the essence of the seller contract
healthy relationship is based on the twin foundation of timely and quality supply on the one hand and prompt and full payment to the supplier on the other
it should be ensured that all payments due to the firm including the central board of indirect taxes and customs in india cbic issues exchange rate notification under the release of the performance security are made on priority basis without avoidable delay as per the conditions as far as possible the payment terms and time schedule should be given in the contract and must be adhered to
any foreseeable payment delays should be communicated to the suppliers in advance prompt and timely provision of statutory certificates to the seller for taxes deducted at source is as much part of the payment as the amount actually released
detailed payment advice showing the calculations and reasons for the amounts disallowed and taxes deducted must be issued to the supplier along with payment
as soon as possible but not later than the date of submission of tax returns the procuring entity must provide the statutory certificates for the taxes deducted from the supplier so that he can claim and refunds from the concerned authorities
as far as msme suppliers are concerned msme act has provisions refer to para for details for timely payments within days and levy of penal interest for delayed payment and conciliation for related complaints by micro and small enterprises facilitation councils
release of payment and settlement of the final bill should be processed through the integrated finance as per the terms and conditions of the contract no payments to contractors by way of compensation or otherwise outside the strict terms of the contract or more than the contract rates should be allowed before the payment is made the invoice should be with the actual receipt of to ensure that the payment matches the actual performance while claiming the payment the contractor must certify on the bill that the payment being claimed is strictly within the terms of the contract and that all the obligations on his part for claiming this payment have been fulfilled as required under the contract
there should also be suitable provision for verification of the authenticity of the person signing the invoice and so on to claim the payment
terms of payment may be decided by the procuring entity safeguarding its interest based on the terms of delivery nature of goods type of inspection mode of transport and risks in such situations
the following payment terms are suggested for various terms of delivery
where the term of delivery is for delivery at site the usual payment term is hundred per cent on receipt and acceptance of goods by the consignee and on the production of all required documents by the supplier
where the terms of delivery are for dispatching station the payment terms depending on the value and nature of the goods mode of transportation and so on may be to sixty to ninety per cent on proof of dispatch and other related documents and balance on receipt at site and acceptance by the consignee
where goods to be supplied also need installation and commissioning by the supplier the payment terms are generally for contract with terms of delivery as for dispatching station sixty per cent on proof of dispatch along with other specified documents thirty per cent on receipt of the goods at the site by the consignee and balance of ten per cent on successful installation and commissioning and acceptance by the consignee for contract with terms of delivery as for at the site ninety per cent on receipt and acceptance of goods by the consignee at destination and on production of all required documents by the supplier and balance ten per cent on successful installation and commissioning and acceptance by the consignee
note generally especially for goods requiring installation and commissioning at the site by the supplier the desirable terms of delivery are for at the site so that the supplier remains responsible for the safe arrival of the ordered goods at the site
therefore unless otherwise decided or for dispatching station terms should be avoided
modes of payment for domestic goods
procuring entities should make payments through the electronic clearance system ecs gross settlement systems rtgs national electronic funds transfer neft or electronic payment gateways
as per rbi guidelines the ecs mandate in rbi format may be obtained at the time of supplier registration and in the tender document
the format is available with all banks
however if ecs payments are not feasible payments may be made in exceptional circumstances by draft drawn on government treasury or branch of rbi or any scheduled commercial bank authorised by rbi for transacting government business
such payment can also be made to the supplier bank if the bills are endorsed in favour of the bank with embossed on the bills with the words received payment and the supplier authenticates both the endorsement and
in addition an irrevocable power of attorney is to be granted by the supplier in favour of the bank
trade receivables discounting system treds is an electronic platform for facilitating the financing discounting of trade receivables of micro small and medium enterprises msmes through multiple financiers
these receivables can be due from corporates and other buyers including government departments and public sector undertakings psus
payments can also be made through this platform to mse suppliers
documents for payment for domestic goods
supplier invoice indicating inter alia description and specification of the goods quantity unit price total value
proof of dispatch railway note
quality assurance certificates manufacturer guarantee certificate or inspection certificate or inspection certificate issued by purchaser inspector
any other document as and if required in terms of the contract
terms of payment usual payment terms unless otherwise directed by ca are indicated below
cases where installation erection and commissioning if applicable are not the responsibility of the supplier hundred per cent net price is to be paid against the production of stipulated documents
in cases where installation erection and commissioning are the responsibility of the supplier eighty to ninety per cent of the net price is to be paid against production of stipulated documents and balance within to thirty days of successful installation and commissioning at the consignee premises and acceptance by the consignee
payment of agency commission if payable against the entire hundred per cent agency commission is paid in equivalent indian rupees based on bc selling rate of exchange after all other payments have been made to the supplier in terms of the contract
modes of payment for imported goods
it should be ensured that the imports into india conform with the policy in force fema fema current account transactions rules framed by procuring entity and directions issued by rbi under fema from time to time
for imported goods payment usually happens through the letter of credit lc refer to para below opened by the state bank of india or any other commercial bank as decided by the procuring entity
the amount of lc should be equal to the total payable amount and be released as per the clauses mentioned above
if the lc is not opened payment can also be made to the seller through direct bank transfer for which the buyer has to ensure that payment is released only after the receipt of prescribed documents
to have uniform payment clauses in gte tenders for foreign and domestic bidders the procuring entity may include provision in its tender conditions on the merits of the case especially contracts for sophisticated allowing payment through lc to domestic bidders also
documents for payment for imported goods the documents needed from the supplier for the release of payment are to be clearly specified in the contract
the paying authority also verifies the documents received from the supplier with corresponding stipulations made in the contract before releasing the payment
documents which the supplier is to furnish while claiming payment are specified in the letter of credit but usually are
supplier original invoice giving full details of the goods including quantity value and so on
certificate of country of origin of the goods to be given by the seller or recognised chamber of commerce or another agency designated by the local government for this purpose
quality assurance certificates certificate of inspection by the purchaser representative or manufacturer test certificate and guarantee
certificate of insurance
bill of receipt or any other dispatch document issued by government agency like the department of posts or an agency duly authorised by the concerned procuring entity indicating name of the bill of bill port of loading date of shipment port of discharge and expected date of arrival of goods any other document as and if required in terms of the contract
air freight charges goods that are required to be airlifted are to be dispatched on forward basis
all air freight charges which are shown on the relevant consignment note as chargeable to the consignee are to be paid to the airline in rupees
some organizations need to import sophisticated instruments tools and kindred goods
these are small in size and very in nature
such goods invariably need to be airlifted
but quite naturally form small part of the air cargo carried by aircraft
for such imports procuring entities may engage air freight consolidators who consolidate the small air cargo of different customers and airlift them from one airport to another
the hiring of airfreight consolidators services should be done transparently following standard principles of public procurement
letter of credit
parties to the lc the purchaser forwards request to its bank called issuing bank in their prescribed format along with all relevant details including an authenticated copy of the contract
based on this the issuing bank opens the lc promising to pay the specified amount to the supplier beneficiary bank based solely on the documents presented by the supplier as specified in the lc conditions without physically ascertaining the shipment of goods
the issuing bank arranges with bank in the supplier region called advising bank to notify the supplier and his bank of the availability of the lc
since the supplier may not be comfortable with the issuing bank it may ask bank he trusts called confirming bank to add guarantee to ensure payments by the issuing bank
risks involved commercial risk due to buyer financial distress
global risk political instability currency fluctuations restrictions disruptions in international logistics
documentary risk discrepancies in submitted documents or interpretation of documents and lc conditions by various parties involved
bank risk bank insolvency or
fraud shipment may not be physically dispatched or dispatched in damaged condition or with inadequate packaging
precautions care should be taken to ensure that all details in the lc such as product description quantity payment terms documents to be produced ld clause and shipping terms are accurate and identical to those shown in the contract to avoid discrepancies
frequent amendments can lead to delays and complications
suppliers may use their own delays in supplies by asking for unnecessary amendments to lc or contract
provisions of uniform customs and practices for documentary credits ucp should be adhered to while opening the lc for import into india
the seller must present documents in time within the tenure of the lc to receive payment and the documents submitted must match the lc requirements
charges and costs opening charges these are incurred by the procuring entity and include both commitment fees charged for the lc validity period and usance fees if the lc allows deferred payment
advising fee this is paid by the issuing bank to the advising bank and is included in charges to the procuring entity
confirming bank fee if applicable paid to the confirming bank by the supplier
amendment fee this fee applies when an lc needs to be extended or amended due to changes in delivery dates terms or other conditions
the party requesting the extension or amendment purchaser or seller pays this fee
retirement charges the supplier beneficiary bank levies these charges on the supplier to handle payment from the issuing bank
other charges reimbursements for foreign trade obligations if any to be borne by the party of that country
for example if there are specific legal requirements related to foreign exchange regulations or documentation in the exporting country the seller may need to cover these costs
if there are specific taxes for foreign exchange remittances then the purchaser may bear such charges
types of lc revocable lc this can be modified or cancelled without notice
irrevocable lc this can not be amended modified or cancelled after issue without agreement and notice to the seller
generally the irrevocable lc is opened so that the supplier is fully assured of his payment on fulfilling his obligations in terms of the contract
confirmed lc an intermediate bank in the supplier country called confirming bank adds its confirmation at the request of the seller guaranteeing that payment would be made as per lc conditions even if the issuing bank or seller bank demurs
unconfirmed lc there is no additional confirmation beyond the issuing bank
transferable lc the seller can transfer part of the lc to another party as payment to his supply chain
lc an intermediary second beneficiary is involved in this
revolving lc this covers multiple transactions over an extended period
it is specifically used for repeated shipments of the same product between the same buyer importer and seller exporter
uniform customs and practice for documentary credits ucpdc or simply ucp is set of rules regarding techniques and methods for handling lcs in international trade finance which has been standardised by the international chamber of commerce the current version being the
deduction of liquidated damages ld the delivery schedule and ld clause including the amount of ld are part of the lc conditions
if the documents submitted inspection certificate and dispatch documents show that these conditions of lc are violated ld as per the lc conditions is deducted from the payment made to the supplier
in case the delivery date of the contract is extended to take care of delay in supply for which the supplier is responsible the tenure of the lc is also to be extended but the expense incurred for such an extension of lc is to be borne by the supplier
advance payment rule gfr conditions for advance payments
conditions ordinarily payments for services rendered or supplies made should be released only after the services have been rendered or supplies made
however in exceptional situations where substantial funds are to be sunk by the contractor before payment becomes due considering the lower cost of funds for the government entity as compared to the higher cost of funds for the bidder advance payment with safeguards bg or insurance surety bond or letter of credit may be considered
so advance payments may be considered only in the following exceptional situations advance payment demanded by firms holding maintenance contracts for servicing of computers other costly equipment etc
advance payment demanded by firms against fabrication contracts contracts or supply of complicated goods and so on
quantum the quantum of such advance payments should not exceed the quantum of funds to be sunk by the contractor before payment becomes due in the contract
the quantum of advance payments should not generally exceed the following limits thirty per cent of the contract value to private firms forty per cent of the contract value to state or central government agency or pse in the case of the maintenance contract the amount should not exceed the amount payable for six months under the contract
in exceptional cases the competent authority may relax the ceilings mentioned above with prior concurrence of the finance
since the provision of advance payment leverages the difference in interest rate as argued in above and considering the additional cost of bank guarantee for advances for the bidder advance payments may be considered with the approval of competent authority and finance concurrence
where an advance is permitted clause in the tender enquiry and the contract may be stipulated that if the contract is terminated due to default of the contractor the advance payment would be deemed as an advance at the interest rate the interest rate of the general provident fund gpf prevailing on the date of release of advance payment plus to be compounded quarterly
in appropriate cases the competent authority may stipulate advance payments with suitable interest rates the interest rate of the general provident fund gpf to be recovered along with the instalments of recovery of advance payment
instalments the advance payment should not be made in less than two instalments as per the expected infusion of funds required in the contract except in exceptional circumstances for the reasons to be recorded
this will keep check on contractor misutilisation of full advance when the contract is delayed considerably
recovery advance payments especially advances should be recovered from either running bills or from the advance payment bank guarantees in instalments linked to milestones or specified periods whichever is earlier
this would ensure that even if the contractor is not executing the work or executing it at slow pace recovery of advance could commence and the scope for misuse of such advance could be reduced
bank guarantee while making any advance payment as above adequate safeguards in the form of bank guarantee or guarantee of at least of advance should be obtained from the firm
in case the advances are to be recovered in instalments an equal number of part bgs with proportionate amount and validity may be taken instead of lumpsum bg with each bg released after related recovery is made
an indemnity bond is not to be considered in place of bank guarantee
however no bank guarantee should be insisted in case advance is being given to central department there subordinate offices or the autonomous bodies attached with them
the bg may also not be taken wherever contract has been placed on cpse on nomination basis
stage payments or part payments against proof of dispatch documents should not be considered as advance payments for the purpose of this para as these payments are made after the sinking of funds by the contractor for achieving these dispatches
these should be provisioned in the tender contract including bank guarantee to be taken if any in case of stage payments
provision of advance payment should be anticipated at the procurement planning stage
the quantum of advance payment and related conditions should be declared in the tender documents with the approval of competent authority and concurrence of integrated finance
if not so declared the condition of advance payment for particular bid should not be agreed to
documents for advance payments documents needed from the supplier for advance payment release are to be clearly specified in the contract
the paying authority should also verify the documents received from the supplier with corresponding stipulations made in the contract before releasing the payment
insurance in every case where advance payment or payment against dispatch documents is to be made or lc is to be opened the condition of insurance should invariably be incorporated in the terms and conditions
wherever necessary the goods supplied under the contract shall be fully insured in freely convertible currency against loss or damage incidental to manufacture or acquisition transportation storage and delivery in the manner specified in the contract
if considered necessary insurance may cover all risks including war risks and strike clauses
the amount to be covered under insurance should be sufficient to cover the overall expenditure incurred by the procuring entity for receiving the goods at the destination
where delivery of imported goods is required by the purchaser on ddp basis the supplier shall arrange and pay for insurance making the purchaser the beneficiary
where delivery is on basis insurance shall be the responsibility of the purchaser
prices the prices should be arrived at independently without restricting competition any consultation communication or agreement with any other bidder or competitor
without undue profiteering the price quoted by bidder shall not be higher than the controlled price fixed by law for the goods if any or where there is no controlled price it shall not exceed the prices or contravene the norms for fixation of prices if any laid down by government or where the government has fixed no such prices or norms it shall not exceed the price appearing in any agreement if any relating to price regulation by any industry
in any case save for special reasons stated in the bid if any the price charged shall not be higher than the maximum retail price mrp
if the price quoted is higher than the controlled price in the above the bidder shall specifically mention this fact in his bid giving reasons for quoting higher price
if he fails to do so or makes any misstatement it shall be lawful for the procuring entity either to revise the price at any stage to bring it in conformity with the above or to terminate the contract for default as per the contract and avail all the remedies available therein in addition to other punitive actions for violation of code of integrity
price components the price schedule should show all the specified components of prices
the price components for goods offered from india and those offered from abroad should be indicated separately in the applicable price schedules
the components should include as applicable gst transportation insurance and price of incidental services as and if mentioned in the schedule of requirements
for goods offered from abroad the price components indicating the currency in the case of gte should include customs duty marine insurance freight and agency commission as applicable
fixed price contracts where the delivery period does not extend beyond twelve months should normally be concluded on firm and fixed price and not subject to variation on any account by inviting tenders accordingly
variable price in tenders with deliveries longer than twelve months price variation clause pvc may be provided to protect the purchaser interests particularly for more than rupees three crore procurements
however even for shorter deliveries or lower value the pvc may be stipulated for items with inputs raw material labour etc
prone to price volatility especially for critical or items otherwise there is possibility of the contract failing or the purchaser having to pay higher price if market prices fall
where it is decided to conclude the contract with variable price an appropriate clause incorporating suitable price variation formula to take care of the changes in the input cost of labour material and power components should be provided in the tender documents to calculate the price variation between the base level and delivery date
it is best to proactively provide our own pvc formula and base dates of indices in the tender document to discourage different bidders from quoting different formulae and different base dates which may lead to problems in bringing their prices on common comparable footing
the variations are to be calculated periodically usually quarterly by using indices published by chambers of metal exchange any other neutral and fair source of indices
suitable weights are to be assigned to the applicable elements that is fixed overheads and various applicable inputs labour for which reliable indices are available in the price variation formula
