yours truly authorised officer enclosure agreement form along with the delivery schedule annexure example of formula for price variation clause refer para the formula for price variation should ordinarily include fixed element and input elements material labour other inputs fuel etc
may also be added if relevant
the figures representing the material element and the labour element should reflect the corresponding proportion of input costs while the fixed element may range from to ten to per cent
the portion of the price represented by fixed element includes fixed costs and profits and is not subject to variation
the portions of the price represented by the material element and labour element along will attract price variation in proportion to their relative share in total cost
the formula for price variation will thus be where pa is then adjustment amount payable to the supplier minus figure will indicate reduction in the contract price on the date of supply
po is the contract price assumed to be price prevailing on the base date date of last deadline for submission of bids but is based on indices prevailing on dates prior to this date as explained in and below
is the weightage of fixed element not subject to price variation as percentage of the total price
is the weightage of the material element as percentage of the total price
is the weightage of the labour element as percentage of the total price
and being percentages should total
it is important that these weightages especially of elements fuel which are known to only become costlier should match the actual content of goods otherwise pvc may result in excessive profit or loss to the bidder
lo and are the average wage indices for the quarter before the respective quarters in which base date and date of supply falls respectively
for example for tender with deadline of submission on march and date of supply is september lo would be average wage index for the quarter of and would be average wage index for the quarter of
and are the material as average of the month specified number of months time lag say two months prior to the month in which base date falls and average of the month two months prior to the month in which date of supply falls respectively
for example for tender with deadline of submission on march and date of supply is september mo would be as average of the month of january and would be as average of the month of july
all material will be basic prices without excise duty and without any other central state local taxes and duties and octroi
if more than one major item of material is involved the material element can be broken up into two or three components such as mx my mz
the following conditions would be applicable to price adjustment
there is period between the date of base date respectively and the dates on which prices are to be considered as per above formula
this time lag can be few weeks prior to such base date of supply depending on the frequency of availability of prices and the supply chain process of manufacturing
this must be specified in the definitions of and indices in the formula in the tender document as above
base date shall be assumed to be the date of last deadline of submission of bids
no price increase is allowed beyond original delivery period
no price adjustment shall be payable on the portion of contract price paid to the seller as an payment after the date of such payment
no price adjustment shall be payable if this is less than or equal to two per cent of po
only materials directly used in manufacture should be included in pvc
other materials used in running of production machines or factory indirect materials should not be included
the total adjustment will be subject to maximum ceiling of to be specified in the tender document beyond which the price variation would be capped at this level
as soon as it comes to light that price variations are likely to go beyond this ceiling and if the supplier is not agreeable to the price variation being capped at that level he may notify the purchaser under frustration of contract provisions in the tender clause for termination of the contract
payments for each supply would initially be made as per the base price mentioned in the contract
price adjustment bills should be submitted only quarterly for the supplies made during the quarter
in gte tenders extra care should be taken when selecting the price indices
preferably the price indices should be from the same country and of the same currency as the country and currency of the bidder
in case the price is in the currency of country where inflation is low and the indices are from country with much higher inflation rates where is the exchange rate of country of and indices with reference to currency of price for example if are from india and is in then eo is number of rs

how to calculate local content
answer para of the order as amended on defines local content as local content means the amount of value added in india which shall unless otherwise prescribed by the nodal ministry be the total value of the item procured excluding net domestic indirect taxes minus the value of imported content in the item including all customs duties as proportion of the total value in percent
mathematically local content sale price value of imported content sale price where sale price means price excluding net domestic indirect taxes and value of imported content means price of imported content inclusive of all customs duties question
how to calculate local content in bids involving supply of multiple items from single bidder
answer in case of bids requiring supply of multiple items say and by single bidder the local content in the bid shall be local content sale price of value of imported content in sale price of value of imported content in sale price of value of imported content in sale price of sale price of sale price of question
how to obtain make in india mii certificate
answer no such certificate issued by government of india
as per para of order as amended on the bidders are required to self certify the local content in their product for purchase value less than crore
for purchases more than crore as per para of order certificate from the statutory auditor or cost auditor of the company in the case of companies or from practicing cost accountant or practicing chartered accountant in respect of suppliers other than companies is required to be submitted
what is the meaning of local supplier local supplier and supplier
answer order as amended on classifies the suppliers into following categories
local supplier suppliers offering items with equal to or more than local content
local supplier suppliers offering items with equal to or more than but less than local content supplier suppliers offering items with less than local content nodal departments are authorized to notify higher minimum local content requirement for any item higher than if they deem fit question
details of product categories for which nodal ministry have been notified by dpiit for mii order may be provided
answer dpiit has notified nodal ministries for different product categories
the details of such product categories and associated department are available on dpiit website
refer link question
can an item be procured from suppliers if there are no local suppliers in the country
answer suppliers can only participate in global tender enquiry
against national tenders only and local suppliers can participate in the bidding process
hence in case item is not available locally from local suppliers global tender enquiry may be floated for procuring item after taking approval of competent authority as notified by department of expenditure under rule iv of gfr
are provisions of order applicable only in procurement of the items for which nodal ministries have been notified and the items for which nodal ministries have issued local content notification
the provisions of order are applicable on procurement of all the items by central government procurement entities
for the items for which nodal ministries have not been designated and the items for which nodal ministries have not issued minimum local content notification the default provision of mii order shall apply
will the cost of transportation insurance installation commissioning training and after sales service support like etc
will be considered as part of local content
answer the cost of transportation insurance installation commissioning training and after sales service support like etc
will not be taken into account for calculating local content in any item
dpiit om part dated refers available on dpiit website
can administrative ministries grant relaxation for procurement of imported items with the approval of hon ble minister under para of order
answer procurement of imported item is governed by rule iv of gfr
hon ble minister of administrative ministry is not the appropriate authority for any in gfr
as such procuring entities are advised to follow the procedures as prescribed in gfr rule iv for procurement of imported items
in this regard minutes of standing committee meeting held on issued by dpiit refers
agenda point number
can administrative give exemption for wide range of product categories for an extended period of time under para of mii order with the approval of hon ble minister charge
answer the administrative departments shall grant only tender specific exemptions under para of the order
exemptions granted shall remain valid for period of maximum year only
if the same items are procured again within the aforesaid period of fresh approval of charge is not required
if any administrative department intends to grant exemption beyond period of year it shall do so only with prior written concurrence of concerned nodal ministry
how do apply for dpiit registration under rule xi gfr for entities having beneficial ownership in land border sharing countries
answer the application format for registration of bidders under rule xi gfr is available on dpiit website
refer link applicants are required to submit one hard copy in the prescribed format along with soft copy pdf as detailed in the covering letter of the format
the applicant shall be asked to submit additional hard copies if required at the later stage

for local supplier the local content requirement is minimum

glimepiride annexure integrity pact format refer para integrity pact between the procuring organisation hereinafter referred to as the principal and hereinafter referred to as the preamble the principal intends to award for under laid down organisational procedures the principal values full compliance with all relevant laws of the land rules regulations economical use of resources and fairness transparency in its relations with its bidder and or contractor
to achieve these goals the principal shall appoint independent external monitors iems who shall monitor the tender process and the execution of the contract for compliance with the abovementioned principles
section commitments of the principal the principal commits itself to take all measures necessary to prevent corruption and to observe the following principles
no employee of the principal personally or through family members shall in connection with the tender for or the execution of contract demand take promise for or accept for self or third person any material or immaterial benefit which the person is not legally entitled to
the principal shall treat all bidder with equity and reason during the tender process
the principal shall in particular before and during the tender process provide to all bidder the same information and shall not provide to any bidder confidential additional information through which the bidder could obtain an advantage in the tender process or the contract execution
the principal shall exclude from the process all known persons having conflict of interest
if the principal obtains information on the conduct of any of its employees which is criminal offence under the act or if there be substantive suspicion in this regard the principal shall inform the chief vigilance officer and in addition shall initiate disciplinary proceedings
section commitments of the bidder contractor the bidder contractor commits themselves to take all measures necessary to prevent corruption
the bidder contractor commits themselves to observe the following principles during participation in the tender process and the contract execution
the bidder contractor shall not directly or through any other person or firm offer promise or give to any of the principal employees involved in the tender process or the execution of the contract or to any third person any material or other benefit which they are not legally entitled to in order to obtain in exchange any advantage of any kind whatsoever during the tender process or the execution of the contract
the bidder contractor shall not enter with other bidders into any undisclosed agreement or understanding whether formal or informal in violation of the competition act as amended from time to time
this applies in particular to prices specifications certifications subsidiary contracts submission or of bids or any other actions to restrict competitiveness or to introduce cartelisation in the tender process
the bidder contractor shall not commit any offence under the relevant act further the bidder contractor shall not use improperly for purposes of competition or personal gain or pass on to others any information or document provided by the principal as part of the business relationship regarding plans technical proposals and business details including information contained or transmitted electronically
the bidder of foreign origin shall disclose the name and address of the in india if any
similarly the bidder of indian nationality shall furnish the name and address of the foreign principals if any
further details as mentioned in the guidelines on indian agents of foreign suppliers shall be disclosed by the bidder
further as mentioned in the guidelines all the payments made to the indian must be in indian rupees only
copy of the guidelines on indian agents of foreign suppliers is placed on annex hereto
the bidder contractor shall when presenting their bid disclose any and all payments made is committed to or intends to make to agents brokers or any other intermediaries in connection with the award of the contract
bidder who have signed the integrity pact shall not approach the courts while representing the matter to iems and shall wait for their decision
the bidder contractor shall not instigate third persons to commit offences outlined above or be an accessory to such offences
section disqualification from the tender process and exclusion from future contracts if the bidder before award or during execution has committed transgression through violation of section above or in any other form such as to put their reliability or credibility in question the principal is entitled to disqualify the bidder from the tender process or take action as per laid down procedure to debar the bidder from participating in the future procurement processes of the government of india
section compensation for damages if the principal has disqualified the bidder from the tender process before the award according to section the principal is entitled to demand and recover the damages equivalent to earnest money bid security
if the principal has terminated the contract according to section or if the principal is entitled to terminate the contract according to section the principal shall be entitled to demand and recover from the contractor liquidated damages of the contract value or the amount equivalent to performance bank guarantee
section previous transgression the bidder declares that no previous transgressions occurred in the last three years with any other company in any country conforming to the approach or with any public sector enterprise in india that could justify his exclusion from the tender process
if the bidder makes an incorrect statement on this subject the principal shall act like para of section above
section equal treatment of all bidders contractors subcontractors in the case of the principal contractor shall take responsibility for adopting the integrity pact by the
the principal shall enter into agreements with identical conditions as this one with all bidders and contractors
the principal shall disqualify from the tender process all bidders who do not sign this pact or violate its provisions
section criminal charges against violating bidder contractor subcontractor if the principal obtains knowledge of the conduct of bidder contractor or subcontractor or of an employee or representative or an allied firm of bidder contractor or subcontractor which constitutes corruption or if the principal has substantive suspicion in this regard the principal shall inform the same to the chief vigilance officer
section independent external monitor the principal shall appoint competent and credible independent external monitor for this pact after approval by the central vigilance commission
the task of the monitor is to review independently and objectively whether and to what extent the parties comply with the obligations under this agreement
the monitor is not subject to instructions by the parties representatives and performs their functions neutrally and independently
the monitor would have access to all contract documents whenever required
it shall be obligatory for them to treat the information and documents of the as confidential
they report to the management of the principal
the bidder accepts that the monitor has the right to access without restriction all project documentation of the principal including that provided by the contractor
upon their request and demonstration of valid interest the contractor shall also grant the monitor unrestricted and unconditional access to their project documentation
the same applies to contractors
the monitor is under contractual obligation to treat the information and documents of the bidder contractor with confidentiality
the monitor has also signed declarations on of confidential information and absence of conflict of in case of any conflict of interest arising later the iem shall inform the management of the principal and recuse themselves from that case
manual for procurement of goods second edition the principal shall provide the monitor with sufficient information about all meetings among the parties related to the project provided such meetings could impact the contractual relations between the principal and the contractor
the parties offer the monitor the option to participate in such meetings
as soon as the monitor notices or believes to notice violation of this agreement they shall inform the management of the principal and request the management to discontinue or take corrective action or other relevant action
the monitor can in this regard submit recommendations
beyond this the monitor has no right to demand from the parties that they act in specific manner refrain from action or tolerate action
the monitor shall submit written report to the management of the principal within to weeks from the date of reference or intimation to him by the principal and should the occasion arise submit proposals for correcting problematic situations
if the monitor has reported to the management of the principal substantiated suspicion of an offence under the relevant pc act and the management of the principal has not within the reasonable time taken visible action to proceed against such offence or reported it to the chief vigilance officer the monitor may also transmit this information directly to the central vigilance commissioner
the word monitor would include both singular and plural
section pact duration this pact begins when both parties have legally signed it
it expires for the contractor months after the last payment under the contract and for all other bidders months after the contract has been awarded
any violation of the same would entail disqualifying the bidders and exclusion from future business dealings
if any claim is made lodged during this time the same shall be binding and continue to be valid despite the lapse of this pact as specified above unless it is discharged determined by the management of the principal
section other provisions this agreement is subject to indian law
the place of performance and jurisdiction is the place from where the contract is issued
changes supplements and termination notices must be submitted in writing
side agreements have not been made
if the contractor is partnership or consortium this agreement must be signed by all partners or consortium members
should one or several provisions of this agreement turn out to be invalid the remainder of this agreement remains valid
in this case the parties shall strive to come to an agreement according to their original intentions
issues like warranty guarantee shall be outside the purview of iems
in the event of any contradiction between the integrity pact and its annex the clause in the integrity pact shall prevail
place date witness witness name address for on behalf of the principal for and on behalf of contractor office seal to integrity pact guidelines for indian agents of foreign suppliers refer section of annexure there shall be compulsory registration of agents for all global tender enquiries gte and limited tender enquiries lte
an agent not registered with the procuring entity shall apply for registration with them
registered agents shall file an authenticated photostat copy duly attested by notary certificate of the principal confirming the agency agreement and giving the status being enjoyed by the agent and the retainer ship being paid by the principal to the agent before the placement of an order by the procuring entity
wherever the indian representatives have communicated on behalf of their principals and the foreign parties have stated that they are not paying any commission to the indian agents and the indian representative is working based on salary or as retainer written declaration to this effect should be submitted by the party principal before finalising the contract
disclosure of particulars of representatives in india if any
bidders of foreign nationality shall furnish the following details in their offer the name and address of the in india if any and the extent of authorisation and authority given to commit the principals
if the is foreign company it shall be confirmed whether it is real functioning company and details of the same shall be furnished
the amount of included in the quoted price for such in india
confirmation of the bidder that the remuneration if any payable to his in india may be paid by the procuring entity in indian rupees only
bidders of indian nationality shall furnish the following details in their offers the name and address of the foreign principals indicating their nationality as well as their status whether manufacturer or agents of manufacturer holding the letter of authority of the principal specifically authorising the agent to make an offer in india in response to tender either directly or through the
the amount of included in the price quoted by the bidder for himself
confirmation of the foreign principals of the bidder that the if any reserved for the bidder in the quoted price may be paid by the procuring entity in india in equivalent indian rupees on satisfactory completion of the project or supplies of stores and spares in case of operation items
in either case in the event of the contract materialising the payment terms shall provide for payment of the commission if any payable to the in india in indian rupees on expiry of days after the discharge of the obligations under the contract
failure to furnish correct and detailed information as called for in paragraph above shall render the concerned bid liable to rejection or in the event of contract materialising the same liable to termination by the procuring entity
besides this there would be penalty of banning business dealings with the procuring entity or damage or payment of named sum
to integrity pact extract of standard operating procedure refer para
the pact essentially envisages an agreement between the prospective and the buyer committing the of both sides not to resort to any corrupt practices in any of procurement process and the contract
only those who commit themselves to such pact with the buyer would be considered competent enough to participate in the tender process
in other words entering into this pact would be an eligibility criterion
the essential ingredients of the pact include promise on the part of the procuring entity to treat all bidders with equity and reason and not to seek or accept any benefit that is not legally available promise on the part of bidders not to offer any benefit to the employees of the procuring entity not available legally promise on the part of bidders not to enter into any undisclosed agreement or understanding with other bidders with respect to prices specifications certifications subsidiary contracts etc promise on the part of bidders not to pass any information provided by principal as part of business relationship to others and also not to commit any offence under prevention of corruption act or indian penal ipc foreign bidders are to disclose the name and address of agents and representatives in india and indian bidders are to disclose their foreign principals or allied firms bidders to disclose the payments to be made by them to agents brokers or any other intermediary bidders are to disclose any transgressions with any other government organization that may impinge on the principle
the date of such transgression for the purpose of disclosure by the bidders in this regard would be the date on which the competent authority took cognizance of the said transgression
the period for which such transgression are to be reported by the bidders shall be the last three years to be reckoned from the date of bid submission
the transgression for which cognizance was taken even before the specified period of three years but is pending conclusion shall also be reported by the bidders
please refer to para of the goods manual
any violation of the integrity pact would be considered as violation of the code of integrity para of the goods manual and would entail punitive provisions thereof para of the goods manual including disqualification of the bidders and exclusion from future business dealings as per the of gfr pc act and other financial guidelines as may be applicable to the organization concerned
the integrity pact would be implemented through panel of independent external monitors iems
all organisations are called upon to make sincere and sustained efforts to imbibe the spirit and principles of the integrity pact and ensure its effective implementation
the final responsibility for implementing integrity pact vests with the head of
the procurement wing of the organisation would be the focal point for the implementation of the integrity pact
the provision for the integrity pact as per annexure is to be included in all requests for documents issued in future in respect of the procurements that meet the criteria laid down in para of the goods manual
in all tenders covered under the integrity pact the particulars of all iems including their email ids should be mentioned instead of the details of single iem
through an appropriate provision in the tender document it must be ensured that the integrity pact is deemed as part of the contract so that its conditions bind the parties concerned
clause should be included in the integrity pact that person signing the integrity pact shall not approach the courts while representing the matters to iems and they shall await their decision
in the case of joint venture all the partners of the joint venture should sign the integrity pact
in the case of the principal contractor shall take responsibility for the adoption of the integrity pact
it is to be ensured that all also sign the integrity pact
in the case of this law has been replaced by bhartiya nyaya sanhita bns from july to integrity pact extract of standard operating procedure contractors the integrity pact shall be arrangement to be signed by the organization the contractor and the
with respect to particular contract the integrity pact shall be operative from the date both parties sign it
appointment of iems integrity pact would be implemented through panel of independent external monitors iems nominated by cvc at an organisation request from its list of empanelled iems
three iems shall be appointed for maharatna and navratna pses and two iems shall be nominated in all other organisations
the iems appointed should be eminent persons of high integrity and reputation
periodical notice inviting applications from eligible persons shall be published on the cvc website
after due scrutiny and verification of the applications and accompanying documents as may be deemed appropriate the name would be included in the panel for nomination as iem
the zone of consideration of eminent persons for empanelment as iems would consist of officers who have held the post of additional secretary to govt of india or were in the equivalent or higher pay scale at the time of retirement whether serving with govt of india or any state govt
ii persons who held the cmd post of schedule public sector enterprise and were equivalent to additional secretary to govt of india at retirement
iii persons who have held the post of and ceo of public sector banks insurance companies and other financial institutions at retirement
iv chief executive officer of an organisation other than listed above and were equivalent or higher to additional secretary to govt of india at the time of retirement
armed forces officers in the pay scale equivalent or higher to additional secretaries to govt of india at retirement
vi the age of iem should not be more than years at the time of appointment
vii if retired person has accepted assignment either in the government sector private sector or elsewhere he shall not be eligible to be on the panel of iems
all those empanelled persons who accept assignments elsewhere would cease to remain on the panel from the date they have taken the assignment
in this regard it would be incumbent upon the empanelled persons to immediately inform cvc about the acceptance of assignment by them
viii all iems should sign agreements with the organisation in which they are appointed
ix person acting as an iem shall not be debarred from taking up other assignments such as consultancy with other organisations or agencies subject to his declaring that their additional assignment does not involve any conflict of interest and is not assignment
the iems must also sign declaration of absence of conflict of interest with existing assignments
in case of any conflict of interest arising later from an entity wherein he is or has been consultant the iem should inform the ceo and recuse themselves from that case
person may be appointed as an iem in maximum of three organisations at time
an empanelled person can not be appointed in one organisation for over three years
role of iems in integrity pact contracts bidders authorised representative may to iems related to any discrimination on account of lack of fair play in modes of procurement and tendering systems tendering method eligibility conditions bid evaluation criteria commercial terms conditions choice of etc
the entire panel of iems should examine the matter jointly who would investigate the records conduct an examination and submit their joint recommendations to the management of the procuring entity
if the entire panel is unavailable for unavoidable reasons the available iem shall examine the complaints
consent of the iem who may not be available shall be taken on record
the iems would be provided access to all of the tender for which complaint or issue is raised before them as and when warranted
the role of iem is advisory and the advice of iem is on the organization however their advice would help properly implement the integrity pact
iem should examine the process integrity they are not expected to concern themselves with fixing the responsibility of officers
iems should not associate cvo and the officials of the vigilance wing during the examination of the complaints in any manner
matter being examined by the iems can be separately investigated by the cvo if complaint is received or directed to them by the cvc
systemic improvements the procurement wing of the organisation shall hold quarterly meetings with the iems
summary of contracts awarded in the previous quarter covered under the integrity pact shall be shared with the iems during the quarterly meeting
such summary of contracts should include details like tender number mode of tendering the period allowed for publicity number of bids received number of bidders considered eligible and name and address of the successful bidder
the above summary of contracts is to help the iems in analysing whether an appropriate mode of tendering is being adopted by the organisation limited tender mode or nomination mode is not unduly used the number of bidders is not too low large number of bidders are not excluded while judging the eligibility or during the technical bid evaluation stage and whether particular firm or set of specific firms is repeatedly getting contracts etc
based on their analysis the iems can suggest to the management suitable systemic improvement and measures to improve objectivity in making capacity building etc
it would be desirable to have structured meetings of the iems with the chief executive of the organization on basis to discuss and review the information on tenders awarded during the preceding period
additional such meetings however can be held as per requirement
all such meetings with the procurement wing or with the organisation chief executive should be minuted
dispute mediation in case of any dispute between the management and the contractor relating to those contracts where an integrity pact is applicable in case both the parties are agreeable they may try to settle the dispute through mediation before the panel of iems in manner
if required the organisations may adopt any mediation rules for this purpose
however no more than five meetings shall be held for dispute resolution
both parties shall equally share the on dispute resolution
if the dispute remains unresolved even after mediation by the panel of iems the organisation may take further action as per the terms conditions of the contract
entitlements of iems iems shall be paid fees of per sitting subject to maximum of in calendar year for the sitting fees
the travel and stay arrangements for the iems for such meetings shall equal their entitlements at retirement
booking travel tickets as per the mode of travel indicated by the iem in writing including email the organisation shall do local transport and stay
the organisation concerned shall provide place for meetings and secretarial assistance to iems for rendering their job
no payment instead of secretarial aid shall be paid to the iems
as mentioned above the stay arrangements and fees for meetings held by iems for mediation between the management and the contractor shall be the same but in addition to the fees for the regular meetings and would be over and above the ceiling of as per calendar year

yes out of target of annual procurement from mses not in the specific tender target of of annual procurement from mses is earmarked for procurement from mses owned by scheduled caste sc scheduled tribe st entrepreneurs and of annual procurement from mses is earmarked for procurement from mses owned by women entrepreneur
however in event of failure of such mses to participate in tender process or meet tender requirements and price for procurement earmarked for mses owned by entrepreneurs and earmarked to women entrepreneur will also be met from other mses
question who is eligible for availing the benefits under the public procurement policy
as mentioned in section of ministry of msme notification no
dated june an enterprise registered with any other organization under the ministry of msme shall register itself under udyam registration
with effect from mses registered under udyam registration are eligible to avail the benefits under the policy
mses registered under udyog aadhaar memorandum uam validity of which is till are also eligible to avail the benefits under the policy
question what is the date of implementation of the policy
the policy is applicable with effect from and became mandatory with effect from onwards
question is the policy transparent competitive and cost effective
the policy rests upon core principles of competitiveness adhering to sound procurement practices and execution of orders for supply of goods and services in accordance with system which is fair equitable transparent competitive and cost effective
question is the policy implemented in parts or fully from its inception
as per gazette notification
dated november it is mandatory for all central government ministries cpses to procure at least of their annual procurement from mses including from mses owned by entrepreneur and from mses owned by women entrepreneur
question is there any monitoring system for assessing the government procurement from mses
to monitor the progress of procurement by central government departments and cpses from mses ministry of msme has launched the msme sambandh portal on december for uploading procurement details by all cpses on monthly and an annual basis which is regularly monitored by the ministry
question is there price matching facility for procurement from mses over large scale
price quotation in tenders in tender participating micro and small enterprises quoting price within price band of per cent shall also be allowed to supply portion of requirement by bringing down their price to price in situation where price is from someone other than micro and small enterprise and such mse shall be allowed to supply up to per cent of total tender value
ii in case of more than one such micro and small enterprise the supply shall be shared proportionately to tendered quantity
annexure faqs about public procurement policy for mses order question what steps are to be taken by the central government cpses to develop mse vendors to achieve their targets for mses procurement
the central government public sector undertakings shall take necessary steps to develop appropriate vendors by organizing vendor development programmes vdps or meets focused on developing mses for procurement through the gem portal
to develop vendors belonging to mses for public procurement policy the ministry of msme is regularly organizing state level vdps and national level vdps under the procurement and marketing support scheme
question what steps are to be taken by the central government cpses to develop vendors from mses owned by entrepreneurs
for enhancing the participation of mses owned by scs women in government procurement central government ministries departments cpses must take the following steps
special vendor development meets would be conducted by cpses for and women
outreach programmes will be conducted by national small industries corporation nsic to cover more and more mses from under its schemes of consortia formation and iii
nsic would open special window for sts under its single point registration scheme sprs
national hub scheme was launched in october for providing handholding support to entrepreneur which is being coordinated implemented by the nsic under this ministry
question what are the other benefits available to the mses under the policy
to reduce transaction cost of doing business mses will be facilitated by providing them tender sets free of cost exempting mses from payment of earnest money deposit adopting to bring in transparency in tender process
however exemption from paying of performance bank guarantee is not covered under the policy
mses may also be given relaxation in prior turnover and prior experience criteria during the tender process
question is there any review mechanism for monitoring and reviewing of the policy
review committee has been constituted under the chairmanship of secretary ministry of msme for monitoring and reviewing of public procurement policy for mses
this committee will inter alia review the list of items reserved for exclusive purchase from mses on continuous basis consider requests from central government departments cpses for exemption from target on case basis and monitor achievements under the policy
question what is the grievance redressal mechanism in case of of the policy by any government department
to redress the grievances of mses related to of the policy grievance cell named champion portal has been set up in the ministry of msme
question whether there is any kind of purchase that has been kept out of the purview of procurement under the policy
if yes how is the monitoring of the set goal done
given their unique nature defence armament imports will not be included in computing goal for defence
in addition defence equipments like weapon systems missiles etc
will remain out of purview of such policy of reservation
monitoring of goals set under the policy will be done in so far as they relate to the defence sector by ministry of defence itself in accordance with suitable procedures to be established by them

yes the policy is mandatory and notified under the msmed act

policy is meant for procurement of only goods produced and services rendered by mses
however sole works contract are excluded from the purview of public procurement policy for mses

the policy is applicable for all mses registered under udyam registration and udyog aadhar memorandum valid till

no there is no exemption on security performance bank guarantee under the policy

in case of private limited companies at least share shall be held by promoters

the policy is applicable for all central government departments and cpses

no there is no such provision in the policy
question what is the objective of the policy
the objective of the policy is to promote micro and small enterprises mses by improving their market access and competitiveness through increased participation in government purchase
encouraging relationship including product development between mses and public sector undertaking pses
increased share of supplies of mses to central government departments and cpses

question how is the status of enterprises as mses be verified
the status of enterprises as mses can be verified through their udyam registration certificate or uam certificate which is valid till march per notification no
dated manual for procurement of goods second edition in case of any discrepancy or complaint the general manager of the district industries centre of the district concerned shall undertake an inquiry for verification of the details of udyam submitted by the enterprise and thereafter forward the matter with necessary remarks to the director or commissioner or industry secretary concerned of the state government who after issuing notice to the enterprise and after giving an opportunity to present its case and based on the findings may amend the details or recommend to the ministry of msme government of india for cancellation of the udyam registration
question can be considered under the procurement target from mse
yes if subcontract is given to mses it will be considered as procurement from mses
question if mses participate in tender but the procuring agency denies providing benefits under the policy how can the problem be addressed
the problem can be resolved through the grievance cell constituted to tackle such situations and the matter may be referred to the procuring agency concerned to redress the problem
question what are the steps taken by the ministry of msme to promote marketing through gem portal for supply of goods or rendering services from mses to government departments and cpses
ceo gem has been requested to make provision in the gem portal for procurement of goods and services from mses through linking urc
udyam registration portal has facility through which an entrepreneur can opt for linking itself with government gem place by selecting an option on udyam portal
the enterprise will be linked to gem portal and flow of information will start between these two portals
with this facility mses can link themselves with the government procurement system and can participate in government mandatory procurement programme from mses
all cpses have been requested to procure goods and services from mses through gem portal only
the ministry of msme has signed an mou with ceo gem for mobilizing mses for onboarding themselves on the gem portal for supply of goods services from mses
all uam holders had been requested to register themselves on gem portal for supply of goods and services through gem portal

order is an executive order

annexure model certificate to be inserted in tenders restrictions under rule xi gfr refer para
while adhering to the substance of the order procuring entities and gem are free to appropriately modify the wording of the certificate based on their past experience local needs etc
model clauses for tenders including tenders issued manually or any electronic portal including gem
any bidder from country which shares land border with india will be eligible to bid in any procurement whether of goods services including consultancy services and services or works including turnkey projects only if the bidder is registered with the competent authority
further any bidder including bidder from india having specified transfer of technology tot arrangement with an entity from country which shares land border with india shall also require to be registered with the same competent authority
bidder including the term bidder consultant or service provider in certain contexts means any person or firm or company including any member of consortium or joint venture that is an association of several persons or firms or companies every artificial juridical person not falling in any of the descriptions of bidders stated hereinbefore including any agency branch or office controlled by such person participating in procurement process
bidder or entity from country which shares land border with india for the purpose of this order means an entity incorporated established or registered in such country or subsidiary of an entity incorporated established or registered in such country or an entity substantially controlled through entities incorporated established or registered in such country or an entity whose beneficial owner is situated in such country or an indian or other agent of such an entity or natural person who is citizen of such country or consortium or joint venture where any member of the consortium or joint venture falls under any of the above iv
the beneficial owner for the purpose of iii above will be as under
in case of company or limited liability partnership the beneficial owner is the natural person who whether acting alone or together or through one or more juridical person has controlling ownership interest or who exercises control through other means
controlling ownership interest means ownership of or entitlement to more than per cent of shares or capital or profits of the company
control shall include the right to appoint majority of the directors or to control the management or policy decisions including by virtue of their shareholding or management rights or shareholders agreements or voting agreements
in case of partnership firm the beneficial owner is the natural person who whether acting alone or together or through one or more juridical person has ownership of entitlement to more than fifteen per cent of capital or profits of the partnership
in case of an unincorporated association or body of individuals the beneficial owner is the natural person who whether acting alone or together or through one or more juridical person has ownership of or entitlement to more than fifteen per cent of the property or capital or profits of such association or body of individuals annexure model certificate to be inserted in tenders restrictions under rule xi gfr
where no natural person is identified under or or above the beneficial owner is the relevant natural person who holds the position of senior managing official
in case of trust the identification of beneficial owner shall include identification of the author of the trust the trustee the beneficiaries with fifteen per cent or more interest in the trust and any other natural person exercising ultimate effective control over the trust through chain of control or an agent is person employed to do any act for another or to represent another in dealings with third person
to be inserted in tenders for works contracts including turnkey contracts the successful bidder shall not be allowed to works to any contractor from country which shares land border with india unless such contractor is registered with the competent authority
the registration shall be valid at the time of submission of bid and at the time of acceptance of bid
if the bidder was validly registered at the time of acceptance placement of order registration shall not be relevant consideration during contract execution

supply installation testing and commissioning of goods supply installation testing commissioning of goods and training of operators and providing statutory clearances required if any in respect of contracts for supply of goods payment including gst should be made after receipt and acceptance of goods and generation of goods crac consignee receipt and acceptance certificate subject to recoveries if any either on account of short supply or liquidated damages etc
for delay in supply
in respect of contracts for services payment should be made as per periodicity defined in the contract monthly quarterly or any other payment periodicity
payment including gst for the particular payment cycle should be made after receipt and acceptance of the services and generation of service crac consignee receipt and acceptance certificate subject to recoveries if any either on account of short supply sla service level agreement deviations and liquidated damages for delay in supply etc
in respect of contracts for supply installation testing commissioning of goods and training of operators etc
the complete cost indicating basic price gst installation and commissioning charges incidental services training etc
is to be indicated separately in the bid
for installation intensive products the different configurable payment terms will have to be incorporated in gem functionalities depending upon the quantum of installation and turnkey work required
first milestone on delivery of goods to payment lower initial payment if installation scope is very extensive of the basic price of goods along with gst on the goods price but excluding installation testing and commissioning and other charges should be paid after receipt goods and generation of delivery crac for initial payment
this will be issued after physical verification of quantity only but without commitment about quality or functionalities etc
which would be verified after commissioning etc
while creating the bid buyer shall have functionality to define the percentage of payment linked with delivery of goods
second milestone on acceptance after installation testing and commissioning balance to payment of the basic price of goods and charges for installation testing and commissioning and other charges along with gst on these charges should be paid after installation and final acceptance of goods and generation of installation crac to be issued by the end consignee
recoveries if any either on account of short supply and liquidated damages etc
for delay in supply or installation etc
shall be made from the payment due under this milestone
while creating the bid buyer shall have functionality to define the deliverables in this milestone and the percentage of payment linked with this milestone
third and subsequent milestones payment of incidental costs payment related to incidental costs at consignee site towards incidental services such as providing training or other service as per scope defined in the contract to be paid on submission of final crac by the end user consignee
while creating the bid buyer shall have functionality to define the deliverables in this milestone
in exceptional cases buyer may choose to split this milestone as in case of contracts for supply installation testing commissioning of goods bundled with one or more services such as comprehensive maintenance human resource hiring for time periods the payments for goods shall be governed by para iii above while payment for services shall be governed as per para ii above
in case of milestone based payments separate timelines delivery periods for each milestone will be provided
in case of supply and installation contracts the delivery period may be specified by filling up the blanks as under
first milestone for delivery of goods at site months from date of issue of contract with provision for staggered multiple delivery period for same consignee
second milestone installation testing and commissioning etc
of goods months from the date of handing over of site complete in all respect as per contract
third and subsequent milestones incidental services etc
days after installation and commissioning
vi the payments on gem are primarily categorized under two heads through pfms or gem pool account
the detailed instructions for both type of payment system are as under
payments through pfms
the central government buyer the concerned programme division or administrative unit in department will place the contract online after taking prior approval of the competent authority for procuring particular good or service
the contract form will also contain the following fields including fields required for payment related processes administrative approval of the competent authority indicating the designation of the approving authority approval of competent financial authority indicating designation of the officer whether ifd concurrence required
if yes then ifd diary no
date budget head of account and year head as in detailed demands for grants
budget availability as on date amount contract value rs budget to be blocked if expenditure is committed for more than year the details portal should generate liability register for recording payment commitments the format for which is prescribed in rule of the gfr
when these fields are duly captured the buyer will be able to place the contract online
the gem portal will generate sanction order and the contract which will be by the buyer
these documents duly by the buyer will be made available online to the concerned ddo and pao or paying authority as defined in the contract and service provider
the ddo and authority shall have access to the contract online to ensure that the bill is generated at the stage of payment in accordance with the contractual provisions
the gem portal will send the sanction order details to pfms
on issue of sanction order and placing the contract for goods the full amount required from the relevant budget head should be blocked in the pfms
in cases of services amount should be blocked for one payment cycle as defined in the contract
before releasing payment for any cycle the funds required for the next payment cycle should be blocked to ensure availability of payable funds for the next payment cycle
blocked fund will be treated as accrued expenditure by pfms for the fiscal year in question and it will not be withdrawn for any other purpose other than the one for which the amount is blocked
to alleviate the operational issues as well as to ensure optimum utilization of available funds the following is notified vide om no
the provision of fund blocking equivalent to full contract value is applicable only for contracts with delivery periods of up to days
for contracts with longer delivery periods fund blocking of appropriate amounts shall be initiated at date days prior to expected delivery date or on the date of invoice generation by the seller in gem whichever is earlier
in case of of required funds at that point of time both buyer and seller shall be alerted and the buyer the head of department hod the pao and finally up to as fa of concerned department shall be alerted by email and sms by gem
on failure in making available the required funds in the appropriate head of account within days seller has right to decline supply and to seek contract cancellation without any administrative action against the seller
also in such case any delay in delivery by the seller will also become exempt from the provision of liquidated damages
functionality to the blocked funds in exceptional emergency cases with some validations head of department hod of the organization on gem can unblock certain of blocked funds of contract may be upto with the approval of associated finance of the department or the cpse in exceptional emergency cases after giving clear undertaking that he will ensure timely availability of funds and unblocking will not lead to delay payments to sellers
however such unblocking will not be allowed if the seller has already raised an invoice before march of financial year
funds for the relevant fiscal year should be blocked only if the delivery period is such that the delivery is scheduled before the of march of that fiscal year
if the delivery is scheduled in march of that fiscal year or scheduled in the next financial year then fund blocking is optional for buyer in current fiscal year and mandatory only in the next fiscal year in the week of april
should it be necessary to amend the contract such amendment in the contract with due approval of the competent authority and acceptance of the provider wherever required shall be made available to the seller authority on the gem portal
similarly in the event of partial cancellation of the contract the information would be made available to the provider ddo and pao on the gem portal
in that event funds so blocked earlier would be released to the extent of cancelled amount
the programme unit in the shall periodically review the blocked budget to ensure that funds are utilized within the same fiscal year
the performance security if any would be obtained from the provider as per contract and their details would be reflected on the gem portal by the buyer
provisional receipt of stores on gem
on dispatch of goods the seller would enter the dispatch details and date of dispatch and will upload documentary evidence of dispatch against each consignment on gem portal
all these documents and details shall be shown to the consignee on his dashboard and shall also be notified to the consignee on his and on his registered mobile number
the seller shall prepare an electronic invoice on gem portal and shall submit the same to the buyer
gem portal will send an email alert to the buyer on submission of invoice
this invoice will contain mode of dispatch of goods quantity with date and price claimed based on contract
in case services are procured the required data as per contract may be incorporated in the invoice
after actual delivery of goods at consignee milestone achievement such as completion of commissioning or training etc
as defined in the contract service delivery seller would enter the actual date of milestone service as applicable and will upload documentary evidence for the same duly digitally signed
in case of services contracts the service provider will fill up the required data as per the contract such as log sheets and invoice etc duly digitally
immediately upon above entry by service provider regarding delivery of milestone service delivery an alert will be flashed on the dashboard of the consignee and an email and an sms alert will be sent to consignee informing that consignee has to mandatorily acknowledge receipt of milestone service delivery through generation of prc on gem
the consignee should receive the and issues an online provisional receipt certificate prc within hours on to contain basis on the gem portal with digital signature mentioning the date of receipt
from this date of receipt mentioned in prc the period of ten days for right of rejection and return policy would be applicable unless otherwise specified in particular contract in case the consignee does not issue prc within hrs from entry of delivery of milestone service delivery by service provider an alert will be flashed on the dashboard of the consignee and an email and an sms alert will be sent to consignee and buyer informing that consignee must mandatorily acknowledge receipt of milestone service delivery through generation of prc on gem
after expiry of hrs
from the first alert another alert will be flashed on the dashboard of the consignee buyer including hod and an email along with an sms alert to consignee buyer hod informing that consignee has to mandatorily acknowledge receipt of milestone service delivery through generation of prc on gem and if the time limit of hrs expires from the date of delivery of milestone service delivery as per entry made by service provider and if the consignee does not acknowledge receipt of milestone service delivery by generating prc or disputes the same by rejecting receipt it would be presumed that goods have been achievement service delivery has been made to consignee and prc will be auto generated by the system deemed prc
however if the consignee does not issue prc within hrs from delivery of milestone service delivery as per entry made by service provider gem would auto generate unsigned prc considering the date of delivery of milestone service delivery as indicated by the seller as deemed date of receipt for issuance of prc
gem portal shall also send periodic notifications every hrs
to the consignee buyer and the hod about issuance of auto generated deemed prc for next hrs
in case the prc is the consignee shall have the provision on gem to respond back within hrs if the goods have not been received or short received recommending to cancel or the date of quantity in the deemed prc
in case nothing is corrected by consignee on the system it will be presumed that the consignee has nothing to say and the deemed prc will be considered as final for all purposes
if it is found at any stage that service provider has uploaded incorrect information on gem based on which prc has been wrongly auto generated the service provider will be dealt severely and should be debarred by gem for three years
consignee receipt and acceptance of stores on gem after issue of deemed prc the system will start sending an alert on the dashboard of the consignee and an email and an sms alert will be sent as per escalation matrix specified below to issue the crac within days level upto days consignee level and day consignee and buyer level to day consignee buyer hod after verification including assessment of quality and quantity of goods of completion of all deliverables defined in the completion of service for the defined period the consignee will issue an consignee receipt acceptance certificate crac goods delivery installation final crac as the case may be within days unless otherwise specified in particular contract of date of receipt indicated in date of receipt as indicated in deemed prc
the crac would clearly indicate the order milestone service delivery rejected unacceptable milestone achievement service delivery if any reasons rejection including quality milestone service delivery accepted and cleared for payment
however if the consignee does not issue crac within days unless some other time line is specified in particular contract for issue of crac on day from the date of deemed date of receipt of milestone achievement service delivery as indicated in prc gem would auto generate unsigned crac which backed with prc or deemed prc based on seller evidence for the corresponding milestone service delivery shall be taken as deemed acceptance for payments in lieu of the requirement of crac
this will be made available on gem to the seller and also the concerned ddo if applicable and authority
the gem portal would generate unique serial number for crac relating to concerned ddo if applicable authority so that the payments are made seriatim
in case the crac is the consignee shall have the provision on gem to cancel or amend the crac within hrs if the goods have not been accepted or found short received
in case nothing is corrected by consignee on the system it will be presumed that the consignee has nothing to say and the crac will be considered as final for all purposes including payments
after generation of crac the buyer shall prepare advice on gem portal indicating any contractual deductions such as penalties for violation of service level agreement as applicable damages for delayed milestone service delivery etc
which will be used by gem portal to compute the net amount payable for the accepted delivery after factoring in the contractual deduction and generate claims for payments by the buyer
this claim for payment shall be made available to the ddo on gem portal and the requisite data will also be pushed online in the pfms
ddo will log into pfms and generate the bill against the said claims and forward the same to the authority for payment after deducting any statuary deductions including tds as applicable
it is obligatory to make payments without any delay for purchases made on gem
in no case should it take longer than the prescribed timelines
the timelines after consignee receipt and acceptance certificate crac issued and by consignee will be two working days for buyer one working day for concerned ddo and two working days for concerned pao for triggering payment through pfms for crediting to the supplier account
in case of return of bills by authority the discrepancies should be addressed by concerned within one working day and thereafter on submission of bill the pao should also not take more than one working day for triggering payment to the service provider any matter needing resolution will be escalated to the next higher level in each agency buyer ddo and pao where the matter should be resolved within hours
in the entire process time taken for payment should not exceed ten days including holidays
after online of all relevant documents authority shall debit the government account releasing the corresponding payment through to be credited into the bank account of the provider
the payment so released shall be credited to the provider account within hours excluding public holidays by the bank
sms alerts shall be sent to the provider and buyer after the payment is authorized by pao and also after the confirmation of the payment by the bank
the payment authorization as well as payment confirmation details shall be shared by pfms on the gem portal
the authority and ddo shall comply with the provisions of general financial rules for budget implementation
in case of return of bill if necessary by authority it should be made online with all for rejections indicated in one go with the approval of competent authority to the for the needful corrections at their end
the ddo shall also be responsible for issuing tds certificate as per income tax act amended from time to time to the seller after release of the payment to the
the ddo shall also be responsible for deduction of tds on gst as per gst provisions and to deposit the same with the govt as per gst rules and issue form gstr to the person whose tds has been deducted
gem would also have provisions for generating supplementary invoice for of statutory changes in duties and taxes if any as above
provision for all types of should be available through pfms
in terms of the provisions of the information technology act as amended from time to time online documents generated on gem shall be treated at par with documents for release of payment to the provider and no ink signed shall be
the liabilities so created as referred to in para vi above shall be reviewed regularly by the programme unit in consultation with the financial adviser
the consolidated information on the total committed liabilities shall be submitted by the financial adviser to the budget division department of economic affairs ministry of finance for suitably reflecting in the budget estimates for the relevant fiscal year and in the expenditure framework mtef
for all contracts placed through gem the payment through pfms to all service providers must be released online only against electronic bill generated on gem
no offline payment should be made in such cases to avoid double payment
only in exceptional cases such as of the gem platform or long shutdown of internet services at buyer location or similar force majeure conditions such payments can be resorted to subject to the condition that immediately after resolution of the problem necessary entries would be made in gem portal to obviate the possibility of double
payment for entities npae
entity npae is government of india gol not using pfms for its payments of transactions and having their own payment system for making payments against contracts placed for placed by the npae on gem
all npae shall open operate special purpose account namely gem pool account for the purpose of ensuring prompt payment to provider of gem who supply services to the npae through gem
accordingly all the departments including cpses municipalities educational institutions autonomous bodies societies etc
not operating through pfms shall be covered under these instructions
these organisations are hereby directed to open operationalize and operate gem pool account gpa for all procurement
gpa is special purpose bank account interest bearing account opened operated and controlled exclusively by each npae
gem pool account shall be mandatory for all procurement irrespective of value
the gem pool account shall be opened operated and controlled exclusively and completely by the buyer subject to certain restrictions on withdrawals of funds as explained in succeeding paragraphs
the account shall carry interest applicable to current account
such account shall be opened in any scheduled bank having already integrated the pool account with gem
the following are the core elements of gpa that should be incorporated during the opening and procurement stages the npae will open the gpa as savings or current account which will be utilized by buyer through the online integration of bank with the platform owned and maintained by gem spv as per service level agreement sla and solely for procurement of goods and services on gem
the terms and conditions of procurement on gem will be part of the operations agreement between the bank and the npae
the role of the bank will be limited to ensuring operations of the account on the instruction of the npae through the authorized npae nodal officer for buyer
real time details of all operations of the account will be shared by the bank in mutually accepted format to be amended from time to time with the npae only through the gem platform
once transaction specific account is credited with an amount the npae can not withdraw this amount apart from transfer to the designated provider till such time that the transaction is live
any by the npae from this account except for payment to the service provider would be permitted in the following conditions
order cancellation order rejection refund all the above situations would first be required to be flagged on the gem platform for the npae to be able to act accordingly
while procuring goods services through gem the npaes should credit of the projected contract value in case of goods contract in their gem pool account before award of contract
in cases of services amount should be credited for one payment cycle as defined in the contract and before releasing payment for any cycle the funds required for the next payment cycle should be credited to ensure availability of payable funds for the next payment cycle
payment so credited will not be withdrawn for any other purpose other than the one for which the amount is credited into gem pool account
after placement of contract on gem the process for prc and crac will be same for npae category also as indicated in para vi above regarding provisional receipt of stores on gem and para vi consignee receipt and acceptance of stores on gem for pfms buyers
after issue of crac npae nodal officer shall issue an advice without delay to the bank to release actual amount payable to service provider as per terms of contract from the gem pool account
on authorization the bank should transfer the prescribed amount to the provider supplier mapped in the transaction
in case of service level agreement sla breach on the part of the npae in terms of payments to the provider gem will intimate the buyer and bank of the same
post such intimation and on the part of the npae with respect to payment transfer bank will release payments for the delivery of goods at consignee milestone achievement such as completion of commissioning or training etc
as defined in the contract service delivery as notified in the terms and conditions of procurement on gem to the service provider mapped in the transaction
such provision is required to be incorporated in gpa and should be considered as standing instruction from the npae to the bank
the residual amount can not be transferred by the npae in such cases
in case even after days of issue of consignee receipt and acceptance certificate crac auto generated crac the buyer has not initiated the payment process through the gem platform payment trigger will be automatically generated for payment equivalent to of the corresponding milestone service delivery deduced by the system as per crac
simultaneously intimation will be sent to the hod buyer and npae nodal officer for gem regarding the release of payment at their risk and cost in line with the terms and condition and sla of procurement on gem
the residual payment of is to be processed by the buyer within days after adjusting for any statutory deduction and damages failing which after days the same will be released to the service provider automatically through an alert to the bank by the gem platform after statutory deductions and any system know deductions
unutilized funds after closure of the contract and interest accrued on the credited amount will be at the disposal of nominated npae nodal officer who may advise banker for further action as deemed fit
the steering committee on gem of each ministry should monitor the implementation of these instructions regarding operationalization of gem pool account
departments of government of india are accordingly requested to issue necessary instructions to all entities under their control
in case any non pfms entity decides with the approval of their competent authority to have integration of their payment systems with functionality for blocking of funds etc
as per pfms system of payments the payment procedures outlined for pfms in para vi shall be mutatis mutandis applicable to them
currently for unlocking of funds especially during the fag end of the fiscal year buyers need to send emails etc
thereafter gem manually unlocks the payments
gem will automate this entire process

circulation to procuring entities appendices appendix advanced concepts of value for money the concept of value value is management and economics concept
it represents the extent of satiation of person hierarchy of needs by product bought for this purpose
this is subjective and difficult to quantify
this is because different persons or the same persons under different circumstances would have different hierarchies of needs and would perceive different extents of satiation or value from the same product
there are three sources of the value of product
the first source of value is from the functional usage of the product known as use value and the second source comes from the social status associated with the ownership of the product esteem value
this can be shown as the difference between luxury branded pen and disposable functional pen though both fulfil the broadly same function and have the same use value
the luxury branded pen in addition to the use value also has additional esteem value
the third source of value comes from the price that one can get by exchanging or scrapping the product at the end of its useful life
this is called the disposal value
normally when people buy car they consider the estimated disposal value of different choices of models
value is the sum of all the three values
while the value of product covers all components of value over the wol the costs incurred on the product should also take into consideration the total of various elements of costs incurred over the wol of the product
for this purpose future costs are discounted to present value not to be confused with the value we are discussing this is financial discounting concept
for example it would not be prudent to buy cheap car that has high cost of operating
this is called wol lcc or total cost of ownership tco
the last is preferred nomenclature in procurement and is defined as the total of all costs associated with product service or capital equipment that are incurred over its expected life
typically these costs can be broken into four broad categories procurement price
the amount paid to the contractor for the product service or capital equipment acquisition costs
all costs associated with bringing the product service or capital equipment into operation at the customer location
examples of acquisition costs are sourcing administration freight taxes and so on usage costs
in the case of product all costs associated with converting the procured into the finished product and supporting it through its usable life
in the case of service all costs associated with its performance are not included in the procurement price
in the case of capital equipment all costs associated with operating the equipment through its life
examples of usage costs are inventory conversion wastage lost productivity lost sales warranty installation training downtime and so on costs
all costs incurred when product service or capital equipment reaches the end of its usable life net of amounts received from the sale of the remaining product or the equipment disposal value as the case may be
examples of costs are obsolescence disposal and project termination costs
besides the value of product or service the customer also has his notion of the value of particular sum of money
this is different for different people or even for the same person in different circumstances
when the perceived value of product matches the perceived value of the amount of money cost of the product the customer feels he got the full value for his money
this is called the vfm
in procurement the total cost of ownership is taken to evaluate value for money
given the limited resources available to the government ensuring vfm in procurement is the key to ensuring the optimum utilisation of scarce budgetary resources
it usually means buying the product or service with the lowest wol costs which is fit for purpose and just meets the specification
vfm also incorporates affordability clearly goods or services that are unaffordable can not be bought
this should be addressed as soon as possible within the process ideally at the need assessment stage before procurement commences
to address this issue change in the procurement approach specification or business strategy may be required
